They are the externalized manifestation of a clinical strategy Subject has adopted without ever, on record, naming it as such. The suit is a *containment garment.* It announces to himself and to anyone watching that the work has bounds: an office, appointments, cases, billable hours of the soul. He takes referrals from NYPD (informal, through a homicide detective named Flint and later through other contacts he cultivates one beat cop at a time). He runs each case as a discrete file with a beginning and an end.

The "Mr. Knight" period is the first phase in his life in which Subject demonstrates **sustained occupational regularity** outside of military or mercenary structure. Behavioral indicators from this era:

- A consistent residential address (a brownstone-front office in lower Manhattan; intelligence indicates he sleeps there rather than separately, a regression in tradecraft that signals his fatigue with running multiple identities).
- A consistent waking-window in daylight hours; nocturnal operations preserved but no longer exclusive.
- Re-emergence of weight, muscle tone, and grooming consistent with three meals a day and sleep on a near-civilian schedule.
- Reduction in observable substance use (alcohol intake measured at social-drinker levels, no opioid signature).
- Reduction in raw alter-switching frequency; alters increasingly described by Subject — when he speaks of them at all — as *tools* he reaches for, rather than as agents who reach for him.

This period also marks Subject's first documented willingness to be **publicly weird without apology.** He will sit on rooftops in white in broad daylight. He will introduce himself by his alias to civilians and shake their hand. The shame layer that drove the earlier secretive vigilantism appears to thin. Whether this is genuine clinical improvement or merely a new defense — *grandiose visibility as a way of pre-empting being seen* — is one of the open questions in the file.

## 4.2 The Hostile Architecture — Khonshu's War and Subject's Open Break (~2018–2020)

Subject's tentative stability is broken by a sequence of events in which **Khonshu is for the first time framed, in Subject's own internal narrative, as an antagonist rather than a master.**

The triggering material is dense and overlapping: a confrontation with a parallel-avatar antagonist ("Sun King," a man whose pathology mirrors Subject's almost exactly, who is presented as what Subject would have been had he embraced rather than resisted the god); a period of institutionalization at the Ravencroft facility, during which Subject is medicated, restrained, and exposed to a sustained reality-testing assault on the entire Khonshu mythology; and the introduction or rediscovery of additional alters not previously catalogued (including a child-state, "boy Marc," and a state explicitly identified as the *internalized abusive mother*).

The behavioral footprint of this period is the most pathologically florid in the entire file *after* the L.A. era. Subject is observed:

- Speaking aloud to empty rooms, with the cadence of a man being interrupted.
- Self-restraining (handcuffs to bed-frames, tying his own ankles to furniture) before sleep, a fugue-mitigation technique he appears to have developed autodidactically.
- Conducting full conversations with himself in a mirror in which both speakers' voices are recognizably his but pitched, paced, and accented differently.
- Carrying, on his person, a small notebook — observed across multiple eras of the file but most consistently here — in which he writes notes *from one alter to another,* a low-tech inter-system communication protocol that DID clinicians recognize and recommend.

The notebook is one of the most diagnostically rich micro-artifacts in the entire dossier. It is bound in black, fits in a jacket inside pocket, written in three distinguishable hands (block-print, looping cursive, and a hurried scrawl) and occasionally in a fourth (smaller, careful, almost a child's), and contains a mix of grocery lists, addresses, threat assessments, apologies, and what intelligence analysts initially mistook for coded operational traffic and later identified as **internal-system housekeeping.**

The functional climax of the period is Subject's **explicit refusal of Khonshu's larger geopolitical agenda** — the moment, on record, when the god's instructions and Subject's own moral code diverge sharply enough that Subject chooses the code over the god. This is the load-bearing event of his current adult life. Until this point, every reading of Subject's heroism could be re-described as obedience. After this point, it cannot. He has, for the first time in fifty years of in-universe time, **disobeyed.**

The cost of the disobedience is the loss of the unified, externally-imposed structure that had organized his fragmentation. He has to build a new one. The Midnight Mission is what he builds.

## 4.3 The Midnight Mission Phase — Current Operational Frame (2021 to present)

The Midnight Mission is a ground-floor storefront in the West Village — verified address withheld in this segment; cross-reference Annex G — with a hand-painted moon on the door and the words *"To those who would do harm in the dark: he sees you"* lettered below in a font Subject either painted himself or commissioned. Inside: a waiting room with mismatched chairs and a coffee urn that is always on; a consultation office with a desk, two chairs, a filing cabinet, and a window overlooking an air-shaft; behind a door marked *Private,* a corridor descending to a sub-basement that contains armory, training mat, medical kit (suture trays, IV stand, AED, narcotics safe of which the key is held by a third party), and a cot.

The Mission operates as a **walk-in clinic for the supernaturally and psychologically afflicted who have nowhere else to go.** Clientele observed during surveillance windows: a teenage girl being followed by a creature only she can see; an elderly woman whose dead husband will not leave the apartment; a man convinced he is becoming an animal; several individuals presenting with what appear to be ordinary mental-health crises whom Subject does not turn away. He charges nothing. Operating costs are evidently subsidized by remnant Steven Grant assets, the disposition of which is opaque but appears to have been consolidated into a small trust rather than the sprawling holdings of earlier eras.

Subject's daily routine in this phase, reconstructed from pattern observation:

- **Pre-dawn (approx. 04:30–06:00):** Returns from nocturnal patrol via a deliberately varied route that nevertheless includes a 24-hour diner he favors (booth in back, never the same waitress two nights in a row if he can manage it, always orders eggs and rye toast and black coffee, leaves a tip well above the bill). Frequently arrives at the diner already wearing civilian clothes over the suit, the white mask in his jacket pocket. Reads a newspaper — *physical paper,* a behavioral fossil — front to back.
- **Morning (06:00–10:00):** Sleep. Documented to be poor in quality; the alternation between street-violence affect and clinic-counselor affect appears to compress sleep architecture. Observed sometimes to skip this window entirely two or three days in a row, then crash for fourteen hours.
- **Late morning to afternoon (10:00–17:00):** Mission open hours. Subject takes intake. He has developed, in this phase, a *clinical* manner — he sits, he listens, he asks open questions, he does not interrupt, he writes notes in the notebook. The Steven-state appears to be the primary front-of-house identity during these hours; the social grace, financial paperwork, and capacity to talk to strangers without menace are Steven's load. Marc-self surfaces when a case escalates, when violence is implied, or when the client is a child.
- **Evening (17:00–22:00):** Case work, training, weapons maintenance. Sub-basement use heaviest in this window. Subject's weapons preference has narrowed from earlier eras' extensive arsenal to a small, ritualized set: crescent darts (thrown), a truncheon (struck), and the cape itself (used variably as restraint, parachute, and tourniquet). The reduction in armament is itself a diagnostic note — *containment in materiel mirrors containment in identity.*
- **Night (22:00–04:00):** Patrol. Subject's routes are now organized concentrically around the Mission rather than around the wider boroughs of earlier eras. He walks more, drives less; the cab — Jake Lockley's cab — has not been documented in operational use in this phase, though Subject has been observed greeting individual cabbies in a way that suggests Jake-affect is still doing intelligence work that does not require the vehicle.

**Therapeutic posture toward his own pathology.** This is the single most important development in the file. Subject in the Midnight Mission phase appears to have *given up the project of being cured* and replaced it with the project of **being useful as he is.** He no longer aspires to integration. He aspires to coordination. The alters are addressed by name, internally and occasionally aloud; they are negotiated with; their needs are accommodated. Steven gets the books and the suits and the office hours. Jake gets the streets and the moral latitude to be uglier than Marc will permit himself. Marc gets the violence that matters and the ministry to the broken. None of them gets Marlene. (See 4.5.)

This is, in clinical terms, a **shift from a fusion-target model of DID treatment to a cooperative-system model** — the contemporary best-practice trajectory for chronic DID patients in whom fusion is not achievable or not desirable. Subject has arrived at this by instinct and by exhaustion, without (so far as the file shows) the assistance of any therapist whose name appears in the record.

## 4.4 The Counter-Avatar — Dr. Badr / Hunter's Moon

The introduction during this phase of a **second avatar of Khonshu** — a Cairo-trained physician operating under the same patron god, observably sane, observably integrated, observably *not* organized around dissociation and self-loathing — is the most important relational development of Subject's recent life and one of the most psychologically destabilizing events in the entire file, precisely because it is presented as *good news.*

Behavioral data from Subject's interactions with this individual:

- Initial response: open hostility framed as territorial. Subject treats the counter-avatar as a competitor for Khonshu's favor, which is structurally absurd given Subject's *break* with Khonshu — and the absurdity is itself the tell. He has lost the god as master but has not lost the *attachment to being the one who serves the god,* and the existence of a sane peer in that role destabilizes the entire arrangement.
- Secondary response (weeks to months): grudging professional cooperation. Subject permits the counter-avatar to operate at the Mission; defers, occasionally, to the counter-avatar's medical judgment; receives wound care from him without the usual aversion to clinical settings.
- Tertiary response (sustained): a guarded friendship in which Subject is consistently the *less* psychologically healthy party and *knows it.* This is the first peer relationship in the file in which Subject has not been able to maintain the posture of the damaged one who must protect the more vulnerable other. The counter-avatar is not vulnerable. The counter-avatar sleeps well. The counter-avatar prays in Arabic and means it. Subject does not know how to receive this and processes it, predominantly, by mocking the counter-avatar's piety in a tone the counter-avatar correctly reads as envy.

The relationship is the single most likely vector for genuine, durable clinical improvement in Subject's life, and Subject knows it, and resists it in the small ways available to him while not, on balance, sabotaging it. *This is new behavior.* In every previous era, attachments that threatened the dissociative architecture were destroyed within months. This one is still standing.

## 4.5 The Marlene Vacancy

Subject's relationship with Marlene Alraune in this phase is best characterized as **stable estrangement.** She is alive. He knows where she is. She knows where he is. They do not cohabit. They do not, on the record of this phase, share a bed. They speak — by phone, occasionally in person, with a frequency that surveillance can establish as approximately monthly with spikes around anniversaries of significant past events.

The relationship has been re-organized, by mutual and unspoken agreement, into something closer to **kin than to spouse.** This is, by every available indicator, the healthiest configuration the relationship has ever held. She is no longer the woman he disappoints by being fragmented; she is no longer the woman whose presence demands he integrate. She is the woman who knew him in Sudan and is still alive, and that fact alone is doing the load-bearing work that her earlier romantic role could not.

Subject does not date. There is no evidence in this phase of romantic or sexual contact with any individual. The Marlene-shaped absence in his life is occupied by *no one,* and his behavior suggests he has accepted this rather than grieved it. The acceptance reads as another sublimation — the ministry has absorbed the affective register that would, in a less broken man, have gone to a partner.

## 4.6 Death, Most Recent

Subject died again within this phase.

The circumstances — assassination by a long-cultivated enemy whose identity is recorded elsewhere in the file — are less important for present-state assessment than the **manner of the death and the manner of the return.** Subject was killed in the open, at the Mission, with witnesses, in defense of a child client. He did not, by all available indicators, fight to survive in a manner inconsistent with the tactical situation; he chose the position that saved the child and accepted the cost. Behaviorally this is **drive number two and drive number three from the personality matrix collapsing into a single act** — the punishment of harm to the helpless, and the seeking of his own punishment, satisfied simultaneously.

The return, when it came, was not framed as Khonshu's gift. It was framed — by Subject, in his own subsequent statements — as *something he came back from on his own terms,* which is either an extraordinary clinical breakthrough or an extraordinary new delusion or both. The diagnostic implication is the same regardless: Subject has begun to narrate his own survival as a matter of his own agency rather than the god's. **This has never been true before in the file.**

Post-resurrection behavior shows:

- Reduction in observed instances of speaking-to-Khonshu.
- Increase in observed instances of speaking-to-alters.
- Increase in observed *physical touch* with chosen-family contacts (a hand on Frenchie's shoulder, an embrace with the counter-avatar that Subject initiates and breaks off after a measured beat).
- A new and previously undocumented behavior: brief, irregular attendance at a small synagogue in lower Manhattan. He sits in the back. He does not speak. He leaves before the rabbi can greet him. He has gone, by latest count, four times.

## 4.7 The Standing Chosen Family

Currently active in Subject's orbit, in descending order of access:

- **Reese,** a young woman Subject extracted from a vampiric cult and effectively adopted as ward and partner. The relationship is the closest analogue to a parent-child bond Subject has ever sustained. He is observably gentler with her than with any other living person. He has taught her field skills, has refused to teach her others, and has organized contingency arrangements (financial, custodial, supernatural) for her in the event of his death — arrangements he has *never* organized for himself.
- **Soldier,** a Mission staffer / operative whose loyalty Subject has earned through extended exposure and who functions as something between a deputy and a younger brother.
- **The counter-avatar** (see 4.4).
- **Frenchie,** still alive, still partnered (in his own personal life, to a man Subject treats with consistent and somewhat formal courtesy), still on call. The friendship has cooled into something like the relationship between adult siblings who lived through the same war and do not need to discuss it.
- **Marlene** (see 4.5).
- **Gena and her sons,** still operating the diner of long association, treated by Subject as extended family with a regularity that the diner-visit pattern (4.3) partially conceals as routine.
- **Tigra and selected former West Coast Avengers contacts,** maintained at distance, called only when supernatural escalation requires team-tier response.

The chosen-family list is **the longest and most stable it has ever been in the file.** This is the single strongest indicator that the Mission-phase architecture is doing real work.

## 4.8 Current Status — Synthesis

Subject as of the latest verifiable observation window is:

- **Physically:** scarred, lean, in the upper-middle range of his lifetime fitness curve; sleeping poorly but eating adequately; substance use minimal; chronic pain managed without opioid relapse; cumulative cranial trauma load high and probably symptomatic but not visibly disabling.
- **Cognitively:** intact, sharp, capable of sustained planning and clinical attention; pattern-recognition still trending toward apophenia under stress but checked, in this phase, by the discipline of casework.
- **Affectively:** stabler than at any previous point in the file; capable of humor (dry, self-directed); capable of tenderness (Reese, child clients, the counter-avatar when no one is watching); still incapable of receiving mercy on his own behalf without weaponizing it; still organizing his risk-taking around an unexamined wish to be killed in the line of duty.
- **Identity-systemically:** in **cooperative coordination** rather than fusion; alters named, addressed, accommodated; primary front-of-house identity Steven for clinic hours, Marc for combat and ministry, Jake for street intelligence; the more florid hallucinated borrowed-hero alters of the L.A. period have not recurred.
- **Theologically:** in functional schism with Khonshu; serving the *mission* rather than the *god*; quietly returning, in increments small enough to deny, to the Judaism of his father.
- **Operationally:** running the Midnight Mission as a low-overhead, high-trust, neighborhood-scaled vigilante clinic; case load steady; collateral civilian harm at career-low; relationship with NYPD informally cooperative; relationship with the broader hero community cordial-distant.
- **Prognostically:** the trajectory is, against every reasonable expectation given the substrate, **slowly improving.** The improvement is fragile. It depends on the continued existence of the Mission, the continued presence of Reese and the counter-avatar, the continued absence of a sufficiently provocative supernatural antagonist, and the continued willingness of Subject to *not be cured* — to accept the cooperative-system frame as the destination rather than the waystation.

The file's working hypothesis: Subject has, in the present phase, achieved something none of his prior eras predicted he could reach — **a sustainable form for a life that was never supposed to be sustainable.** The form is not health in any textbook sense. It is a man who has organized his madness into a small storefront on a quiet block, opened the door, and put coffee on, and waited for the people no one else will see to come in. He is still, by every standard he himself would apply, not a good man. He is, by the standard the file would apply, the closest thing to one he has ever been.

**End of segment. Continue to Annex A — Routes, Routines, and Tells.**


## Medical History

# UATU DOSSIER — MARC SPECTOR / MOON KNIGHT
## SECTION: MEDICAL HISTORY

*A longitudinal somatic file. Where canon is silent, inference is marked. The body is the primary record; this man does not keep charts, does not retain physicians, and avoids hospitals on principle, so the body itself is the document.*

---

### I. CONSTITUTIONAL BASELINE

**Phenotype.** Adult male of Ashkenazi Jewish descent, paternal line of Eastern European (likely Czech/Polish) Holocaust survivors. Adult height in the 6'1"–6'2" range, frame mesomorphic and overbuilt through deliberate hypertrophy rather than natural mass. Resting body composition cycles between two distinct steady states: a **boxer's lean** (≈195 lb, low single-digit body fat, characteristic of the Marine and active mercenary years and re-attained by the MacKay-era Mission period) and a **wasted** state (≈170 lb, with measurable sarcopenia and pallor, attained during the post-Bushman convalescence pre-Huston and during institutionalizations under Lemire and Bemis). The pendular weight curve over fifty published years is itself diagnostic — bodies of long-term combatants do not normally lose and re-recruit twenty-five pounds of lean tissue on a cycle measured in months.

**Genetic load.** No documented heritable disease, but two relevant family-history items: (1) paternal Holocaust survival, raising the now-established literature on intergenerational HPA-axis dysregulation, baseline cortisol abnormalities, and increased lifetime PTSD vulnerability; (2) the retconned maternal psychiatric history (Bemis, MacKay flashbacks), which raises priors for inherited mood-disorder and possibly dissociative vulnerability. Neither is *medical* in the strict sense, but both shape what trauma did to this organism.

**Vital baselines (inferred from depicted exertion tolerances).** Resting heart rate in the high 40s to low 50s — endurance-athlete range. Blood pressure persistently low-normal in conditioned states, normal-to-high in depleted states (consistent with the autonomic dysregulation typical of C-PTSD). VO₂ max estimable in the 55–60 ml/kg/min range during the West Coast Avengers and Mission-era windows; collapses to sedentary norms during depressive phases.

---

### II. PRE-SUDAN ERA: THE FOUNDATIONAL DAMAGE (boyhood through CIA exit)

#### 1. Childhood somatic record (Chicago, ages 0–~16)

Canonical material from Moench's original origin, expanded in Lemire/Smallwood flashbacks and Bemis's maternal retcons, supplies a child whose body was a battlefield before his vocation chose one.

- **Suspected physical/emotional abuse by mother** (Bemis, MacKay): unspecified injuries plausible — the kind that don't reach a pediatrician. Inferred: bruising in non-impact distributions, possible undiagnosed greenstick fractures of the forearm or ribs, scalp trauma below cosmetic threshold. The somatic record of childhood maltreatment is most often *invisible* — it shows up as adult chronic pain syndromes, lower pain threshold paradoxically masked by higher pain tolerance, and elevated baseline inflammatory markers. All three are observable in the adult Spector.
- **Early aggression toward animals or peers** is *not* clearly canonical and should not be over-inferred; the conflict with Elias is moral and temperamental, not yet criminal.
- **Bar mitzvah-age weight/height progression normal**, but the pivot to boxing in mid-adolescence (Moench origin) suggests early channeling of dysregulated affect into physical contact. By 14–16 he is taking hand-to-hand impact regularly. **First subclinical concussions almost certainly occur here.**

#### 2. Amateur and semi-professional boxing (mid-teens to early 20s)

- **Estimated rounds sparred**: in the low thousands across an amateur run sufficient to draw Marine recruiter interest. At one diagnosable concussion per ~50–100 contact rounds for a power-trading aggressive fighter, the floor estimate for **subclinical concussions sustained by age 20 is 15–30**.
- **Hand damage**: characteristic boxer's-knuckle deformities, healed metacarpal microfractures (the "boxer's fracture" of the fifth metacarpal almost certainly present bilaterally by adulthood), thickened MCP joints, early osteoarthritic changes by his 30s.
- **Orbital and zygomatic trauma**: probable healed orbital floor fracture (the slight asymmetry of his depicted gaze under Sienkiewicz and Smallwood is consistent), recurrent epistaxis, and a deviated septum likely repaired informally. He does not breathe through his nose under exertion in any era — a behavioral tell present from Moench forward.
- **Cumulative subconcussive load**: this is the foundational stratum of his eventual neurocognitive picture. CTE-spectrum pathology does not require knockouts; it requires *frequency*, which boxing supplies.

#### 3. United States Marine Corps service

- Standard combat-arms training: musculoskeletal load injuries (stress fractures of the tibia, plantar fasciitis, lumbar facet irritation — the universal pack-and-rifle inventory). Hearing loss in the 4–6 kHz range from sustained unprotected firearms exposure is essentially certain; he exhibits the characteristic *over-turning* of the head to track speakers in cluttered audio environments (depicted across Huston and MacKay).
- **Combat tour(s)**: locations un-fixed across canon but presumed Middle East / Africa given subsequent contact networks. Likely first kills here. Likely first *moral injury* here (predating Sudan), which matters medically because the cortisol-adrenergic priming for what Sudan would become is laid in now.
- **Discharge status**: not honorable in spirit if not in paperwork; he leaves to do for money what the Marines wanted him to do for ideology. The body keeps no record of motive, but the immune and endocrine consequences of chronic threat exposure begin now and never reset.

#### 4. CIA period (brief)

- Adds tradecraft injuries: at least one suspected fall or vehicular incident producing the chronic right-knee complaint visible in his fighting stance (he favors the left leg as base across all artists who draw stance consistently — Sienkiewicz, Texeira, Finch, Smallwood, Cappuccio).
- Likely first exposure to **interrogation-resistance training**, which uses controlled sleep deprivation and stress-position work — these are *iatrogenic* dissociative inductions and almost certainly potentiated his pre-existing dissociative architecture.
- Exit from CIA is acrimonious; whether or not he was formally burned, he lost institutional medical access here and never regained it.

#### 5. Mercenary years (the unrecorded middle)

- Multiple gunshot wounds, healed and unhealed. The body of the adult Spector, undressed under Smallwood, Cappuccio, and Cabal, is mapped with **stippled scarring**: at minimum a through-and-through of the left lateral thigh, an entry scar at the right lower quadrant (concerning for past visceral injury — query splenic or hepatic involvement, probable laparotomy scar present), a graze along the left deltoid, and a healed clavicular fracture site with palpable callus.
- Edged-weapon scarring across both forearms (defensive wounds), a deep oblique scar across the right palm (knife-grab), and the characteristic asymmetric callusing of the trigger finger and thumb web.
- **Malaria exposure** plausible given African operational tenure — recurrent low-grade febrile episodes in later runs (the "sweats" in Huston attributed to withdrawal could partially be relapsing-fever residua).
- Likely **untreated parasitic and dermatological burden** from desert and jungle work — tinea, occasional cellulitis, possibly latent TB exposure given Sudanese and Eastern African contacts.

---

### III. THE SUDAN EVENT (load-bearing trauma; *Moon Knight* vol. 1 #1)

This is the medical *and* spiritual axis of the file. Reconstructed somatic sequence:

1. **Blunt-force assault by Bushman**: repeated strikes to the head and torso with fists, boots, and probable rifle butt. Acute findings inferable from his depicted state when found: bilateral periorbital ecchymosis ("raccoon eyes" — concerning for basilar skull fracture), bloody otorrhea or rhinorrhea, multiple rib fractures (he holds the left flank for years afterward when winded), probable pneumothorax (small, self-resolving), maxillofacial fractures, and a **closed head injury with prolonged loss of consciousness sufficient to be field-diagnosed as death**.
2. **Hypovolemia and exposure**: dragged or crawled some distance in the desert. Severe dehydration, heat injury (probably moved through heat exhaustion into heat stroke), hyponatremia, acute kidney injury almost certain at the time, likely with full recovery but with permanent reduction in renal reserve.
3. **The "death."** Whether one reads it as cardiac arrest with spontaneous reperfusion, severe hypovolemic syncope, or genuine clinical death with supernatural resuscitation, the **anoxic insult to the brain** is real and large. Hippocampal and watershed-cortical neurons are the first to die in such events; the memory disturbance, the affective flattening between alter-states, and the increasing prominence of Khonshu over the decades are all consistent with what such an insult would, in time, produce.
4. **The recovery at the Khonshu statue** — by Marlene and the Bedouin (later: Selim's people). No surgical intervention; healing by time, bedrest, and whatever traditional care was available. Fractures malunion-set; ribs heal angulated (visible in later anatomical depictions); a small permanent kyphosis at T6–T8.

**Psychological consequence specific to the medical event:** he experiences his own death and credits a god for the resurrection. Every subsequent risk he runs is, neurologically, an attempt to reproduce the only spiritual experience he has ever had. The body has been taught that near-death is a doorway. This is medically catastrophic.

---

### IV. THE FIRST VIGILANTE DECADE (Moench/Sienkiewicz through Dixon/Hama/Platt)

#### Injury inventory, partial:

- **Repeated lacerations** along the standard combat distribution (forearms, scalp, mandible), self-sutured or Marlene-sutured. The characteristic *ladder* of fine white scars along the left forearm.
- **At least two more concussions** of clinical severity per year of active operation, conservatively. Across this decade: **20–30 additional concussions**, on top of the boxing baseline and the Sudan event.
- **A penetrating abdominal wound** referenced in the Dixon era requiring extended convalescence with Marlene.
- **Hand and wrist arthropathy** accelerating; he changes his striking style across the decade from boxing-derived (jab-cross) to a more open-hand and elbow-heavy mix — a behavioral adaptation that is *also* a medical document of joint deterioration.

#### Substance baseline, this era:

- Social drinking, moderate. No documented dependence yet. Caffeine heavy and constant.
- Use of OTC analgesics presumably escalating; introduction of prescription opioids likely begins through black-market or Frenchie-procured channels for the recurring orthopedic pain.

---

### V. THE CRIPPLING AND THE COLLAPSE (pre-Huston, Huston *Moon Knight* vol. 4 #1–6)

The most precisely documented medical phase of his life.

#### The injury

A second confrontation with Bushman ends with Marc's lower body crushed/severely injured (canonically presented as having "broken" him — a combination of pelvic, femoral, and lumbar damage). Depicted post-injury:

- **Mobility loss**, requires a cane and at times a wheelchair.
- **Chronic pain** localized to the lumbosacral and right hip distribution, neuropathic component (depicted dysesthesia and night pain).
- **Disuse atrophy** of the lower extremities and trunk, with corresponding loss of upper-body conditioning over the months of immobility.
- **Weight loss** through anorexia of depression, then weight cycling.

#### The self-medication

- **Alcohol**, heavy and daily. Marlene and Frenchie remark on it; bottles populate his environment in Finch's panels.
- **Opioid analgesics**, source unspecified — almost certainly oxycodone-class or stronger; the depicted nodding, pupillary constriction (where colorists permit), and constipation-adjacent affect-flattening fit.
- **Probable benzodiazepine use** for sleep and the panic phenomena. Cross-tolerance with alcohol obscures the picture.
- **Nutritional collapse**: subsists on what's brought to him; loses muscle, gains a small visceral pad despite caloric deficit (cortisol-mediated central adiposity), develops the gray, thinned skin of chronic substance use.

#### Psychological consequence

This is the period in which the alter system *cannot operate* — Steven cannot move in society as an invalid recluse, Jake cannot drive a cab on opioids, and Marc-self is left to bear the whole affective load without the dissociative outlets that ordinarily distribute it. The result is the most florid psychiatric depiction in canon and a near-total functional collapse. **Recovery is not medical; it is mythic** — Khonshu's recall, the return to violence, the literal carving of Bushman's face. The body is re-recruited by re-purposing it. Detox is unmedicated, brutal, and almost certainly incomplete; the painkiller relapses across subsequent runs are predictable on this basis.

---

### VI. THE BENDIS / LOS ANGELES PERIOD

- Operating at high function but in floridly psychotic dissociative territory (the Avengers-alters).
- **Sleep**: severely disturbed; the borrowed-identity hallucinations have the dream-intrusion quality of severe REM dysregulation and may indicate a parasomnia-spectrum overlay (REM behavior disorder is plausible in a man with this much head trauma).
- **Cardiovascular**: sustained sympathetic activation. Resting tachycardia in calm scenes is depicted. Blood pressure likely creeping. He is, by this point, at meaningful actuarial risk for a cardiac event in his early 50s.
- **Renewed combat injury**: knife and gunshot, including a significant chest wound in this era's climax.

---

### VII. THE ELLIS / "MR. KNIGHT" INTERVAL

Medically the *best* period of his adult life on record. The suit replaces the cape, the cases are contained, sleep stabilizes, substance use appears at functional baseline. His weight returns to lean operating range; the facial swelling of the substance-heavy Huston era is gone in Shalvey's lines. This remission is fragile and is broken by the next reality-failure (Lemire).

---

### VIII. THE LEMIRE ASYLUM ARC (*Moon Knight* vol. 8)

- **Iatrogenic and forced pharmacology**: antipsychotic loading (depicted side effects consistent with first-generation neuroleptics — rigidity, drooling, the masked face), possible ECT (the recovery-room imagery in Smallwood's pages can be read this way), restraint injuries (wrist abrasions, the characteristic posterior shoulder ache of prolonged supine restraint).
- **Cardiovascular event ambiguous**: the "death" sequences inside this arc are dream-logic but include physiological imagery (chest clutch, collapse) that fit a real arrhythmic event masked by the arc's surrealism.
- **Refeeding and reconditioning** on release — he is visibly underweight at the arc's outset and rebuilds slowly.

The medical-psychiatric reading: the asylum did some pharmacologic harm and considerable iatrogenic dissociative injury (forcibly suppressing alters is, in DID care, contraindicated), and he leaves with a worsened relationship to medical institutions that will persist.

---

### IX. THE BEMIS PERIOD

- Further institutional cycling; further unwanted medication trials. He learns the trick of *cheeking* and palming, depicted obliquely.
- Confrontation with the Sun King involves burn exposure — partial-thickness burns to the upper extremities and torso, healed with characteristic hypopigmented scarring superimposed on the existing scar map.

---

### X. THE MACKAY / MIDNIGHT MISSION ERA

The second-best medical period on record after Ellis, and the most *sustainable*.

- **Routine reasserted**: regular sleep windows (afternoon-into-evening, consistent with the operational schedule), regular meals (Reese and the Mission's flow of clients impose social eating), reduced substance load.
- **New injuries continue** — a near-fatal stabbing in the Hunter's Moon storyline, a depicted resuscitation, and the run-closing **death and resurrection** (his third canonical death). Each of these is, again, an anoxic-ischemic insult superimposed on the existing brain.
- **The Hunter's Moon relationship** is medically significant: Dr. Badr is, among other things, a physician, and his presence is the closest thing to consistent medical oversight Marc has had since Marlene. The Mission is functioning, quietly, as Marc's *outpatient clinic of one*.
- **Late-life cumulative toll**: by this era he has the joint exam of a 70-year-old former heavyweight, the brain of a man with documented repeat TBI and three death-events, and the endocrine profile of someone who has lived in fight-or-flight for forty years. He should be far more disabled than he is. The compensations are real and they are running out.

---

### XI. CATALOG OF "TRANSFORMATIONS" AND SUPERNATURAL SOMATICS

Setting aside the question of Khonshu's ontology, the following are *somatically observable*:

- **Lunar-cycle strength variance**: depicted across multiple eras (most explicitly Moench, revived under MacKay). Behaviorally, his risk-taking and pain tolerance peak around the full moon. Whether this is endocrine entrainment, placebo-mythic, or genuinely supernatural, it is a *reliable* monthly fluctuation in his operating envelope and should be modeled as such.
- **Resurrections (x3 minimum)**: Sudan, *The Bottom* / Huston-era near-death sequences, MacKay run finale. Each leaves him neurologically subtly altered — increasing dissociative fluency, increasing Khonshu salience, increased anhedonia in inter-mission windows.
- **The Mr. Knight / Moon Knight / Fist of Khonshu costumes** function as somatic state-changes: heart rate, posture, vocal register, and gait shift on donning. This is *not* mystical; it is well-documented state-dependent embodiment in DID and trauma populations, layered with combat-uniform conditioning.
- **Periods of "Khonshu possession"** (most explicit in Huston and post-*Avengers vs. X-Men* material): behaviorally indistinguishable from a dissociative fugue with full executive capture by an alter, plus the affective fingerprint of the persecutor introject. The "possession" episodes correlate with sleep deprivation and post-injury states — i.e., the conditions that potentiate dissociation in any patient.

---

### XII. CUMULATIVE SOMATIC SCAR MAP (the body as document)

For surveillance purposes a Spector identification could be made on scarring alone:

- **Forehead/scalp**: multiple small linear scars at the hairline; a particular curved scar above the right brow from the Bushman era.
- **Face**: deviated septum; healed left zygomatic depression; fine scarring along the mandible.
- **Torso**: anterior — the laparotomy scar (lower midline), the right-upper-quadrant entry scar, scattered shrapnel and burn marks; posterior — the kyphotic prominence at T7, paraspinal hypertrophy asymmetric to the left, an exit-wound scar at the right scapular border.
- **Upper extremities**: ladder of forearm scars bilaterally, palmar grab-scar right, boxer's-knuckle deformity bilaterally with worse changes right.
- **Lower extremities**: the through-and-through left thigh scar, surgical (or improvised-surgical) scars at the right hip and proximal femur from the Bushman crippling, characteristic right-knee meniscal-scope scars unlikely (he did not have the procedure) but corresponding chronic effusion and crepitus.
- **Generalized**: low body hair burden in scar zones; thermoregulation modestly impaired in the burn-scar distributions; tattoo-absent (a Jewish-tradition retention quietly preserved across runs despite the Egyptian iconography around him — *the body of Elias's son is not marked*).

---

### XIII. SUBSTANCES, LONGITUDINAL

- **Alcohol**: social → heavy episodic (mercenary years) → daily-dependent (Huston pre-return) → variable remission with relapses (post-Huston, Bemis). Hepatic function probably still compensated but reserve diminished.
- **Opioids**: introduced via injury management; documented dependence in the Huston era; periodic relapse plausible. He recognizes the pattern and avoids it but does not always succeed.
- **Benzodiazepines**: inferred, for sleep and panic. Use likely tapered in stable eras.
- **Caffeine**: heavy and constant across all eras; one of the few "substances" he protects.
- **Nicotine**: variable, era-dependent; consistent with mercenary cohort; not central to his identity.
- **Stimulants illicit**: not canonical, and inconsistent with his somatic presentation. The hypomanic Steven-phases are dissociative, not pharmacologic.
- **Antipsychotics, mood stabilizers, antidepressants**: trialed under coercion, never sustained voluntarily; he experiences medication as another form of restraint.

---

### XIV. SYNTHETIC MEDICAL READ

The medical history of Marc Spector is the history of a body that has been used as a sacrificial implement by the mind that lives in it, and that has paid the bill its operator has refused to pay. The most likely cause of his eventual death, absent further supernatural intervention, is one of three: a **cardiac arrhythmic event** on the substrate of decades of sympathetic overdrive and stimulant load; a **fatal CNS bleed** during a routine combat engagement, on the substrate of cumulative TBI and probable cerebrovascular fragility; or a **terminal dissociative-suicidal collapse** in which the operator decides, on Khonshu's instruction or his own, that the body has fulfilled its purpose.

The countervailing fact is that he has *organized his life,* in the MacKay era, into something that supplies the routine, sleep, nutrition,


## Somatic Atlas

# UATU DOSSIER — MARC SPECTOR / MOON KNIGHT
## Section: SOMATIC ATLAS

*The body as longitudinal evidence. What follows is the granular physical record — what a surveillance team watching him for years would notate, cross-reference, and learn to read as a second language. Every entry is keyed, where possible, to the state-shifts that re-arrange it: BASELINE (Marc-primary, undisturbed), STRESS (operational pressure, sleep-deprived, pre-violence), THREAT (acute combat or imminent confrontation), INTIMACY (Marlene present, child in distress, debriefing a victim), DEPLETED (post-violence, post-switch, post-Khonshu episode), and ALTER-STATE (Steven / Jake / others overt).*

---

### 1. THE FRAME ITSELF

Subject reads at approximately six feet, between 195 and 215 pounds depending on era — the weight is *not stable*. Boxer's build adulterated by mercenary years (heavier, denser through the shoulders and trapezius), partially atrophied during the post-Bushman convalescence (Huston run: visibly thinner through the deltoids, soft through the abdomen, palor at the temples), then methodically rebuilt. The rebuild is uneven; he trains the body he needs for tomorrow's fight, not the body of a man with a long view. Right shoulder sits perhaps a quarter-inch higher than the left — old rotator-cuff insult, never properly rehabilitated, masked under the cowl.

**Skin and scar inventory.** Catalogued by region:
- *Forehead and scalp:* irregular keloid above the right eyebrow (Sudan beating); two surgical scars at the parietal (cranial pressure relief, undocumented surgeon, likely Frenchie-era field medicine); minor punctate scars along the hairline from glass and shrapnel.
- *Face:* hairline scar bisecting the upper lip (boxing; visible only when he doesn't shave for three days and the hair won't grow through it); faint silvering along the right zygomatic; nose broken minimum three times, healed off-axis to the left by perhaps two degrees, perceptible only in true profile.
- *Torso:* bullet entry/exit pairs — left flank (through-and-through, abdominal), right pectoral (lodged, scar puckered); a curved blade scar running from sternum to right floating rib (Bushman's knife, the night of the Khonshu encounter); burn scarring across the lower back, mottled, palm-sized; surgical scarring midline (laparotomy, post-death event in *The Bottom* arc).
- *Arms and hands:* knife defensive wounds on the forearms (white lines, parallel, more on the left); knuckle scarring is the most diagnostic single feature on his body — the third and fourth metacarpals on both hands are thickened, the skin over them is permanently darker, the knuckles will not fully close into a smooth fist because of repeated micro-fractures. A surveillance analyst would identify him by these hands in a crowd of strangers, even gloved.
- *Legs:* surgical hardware in the right femur (the period after Bushman crippled him); scar tissue at the right knee that produces a perceptible click on full extension; old shrapnel under the skin of the left calf, palpable, never excised.

The body is a written document. He knows every line on it and has stopped noticing any of them.

---

### 2. GAIT AND CARRIAGE

**Baseline.** Walks slightly toed-out, weight forward over the balls of the feet — boxer's stance never fully unlearned. Stride length shorter than his height would predict; he covers ground efficiently, not gracefully. Hands tend to hang half-cupped, fingers loosely curled, as though always a quarter-second from a fist. Shoulders carried high and slightly rolled forward — a protective posture he developed in the convalescent years and never released. Head tilts perhaps five degrees down, eyes up — the universal posture of a man who expects to be hit and has decided to see it coming.

**Stress.** Stride shortens further; weight drops lower into the hips; the toe-out resolves toward neutral as the body organizes for combat. He stops swinging his arms.

**Threat.** Goes very still before he moves — a full half-second of complete motionlessness in which a trained observer can see the breath leave him, the pupil expand, the weight redistribute. Then the movement is shockingly economical: he closes distance by *gliding,* feet barely leaving the floor, no telegraph in the shoulders. This is the boxer training, refined by Marine close-quarters work, refined again by twenty years of nocturnal violence. He does not bounce. He does not wind up. The first strike is already in motion before the witness has registered intent.

**Intimacy.** Walks heavier, deliberately — he makes noise so as not to frighten. Around Marlene specifically, the toe-out increases (relaxation), and the shoulders drop visibly within the first ten seconds of her presence. Around children, he crouches before he speaks, every time, without exception. This is one of the few automatisms that crosses *all* alters.

**Depleted.** Limp on the right, favoring the old femur; pace slows by perhaps thirty percent; the hand-cupping becomes a fist-clench-and-release cycle, every fifteen to twenty seconds, as he manages pain. He will lean on walls without seeming to lean — palm flat against vertical surfaces as he passes, transferring weight for a half-stride at a time.

**Alter-state — Steven.** Stands a full inch taller. The forward shoulder-roll disappears entirely; the chin lifts; the gait lengthens and gains a measured, almost lazy quality. He occupies more horizontal space — arms freer of the body, gestures wider. He walks into rooms he owns.

**Alter-state — Jake.** Lower center of gravity, more rolling in the hips, weight on the outside edges of the feet (the cabbie's stance — long hours on hard pedals). Hands jam into pockets. He moves *through* crowds rather than around them, with a street-confidence that has nothing to do with confrontation and everything to do with knowing every exit.

---

### 3. THE FACE

**Resting face.** The mouth sits in a slight downturn; the brow carries a permanent low-grade furrow at the medial point; the eyes are habitually narrowed by perhaps fifteen percent from neutral, an old desert-sun adaptation that has become character. He does not have an open face. Strangers report him as unreadable; intimates report him as legible only by absence — they read what he is *not* doing.

**The blink rate.** Below normal at baseline (perhaps twelve to fourteen per minute against an average twenty), drops to almost nothing during threat assessment, *spikes* during alter-switch (a flutter, two to four rapid blinks in succession), and increases markedly during Khonshu episodes — at which point the eyes also track to a fixed point above and to the right of the interlocutor, where the god's presence apparently registers.

**Micro-expressions of note:**
- A brief, involuntary tightening of the masseter when his father is mentioned (Elias, the rabbi, Chicago) — visible as a small bunching at the angle of the jaw. He does not know he does this.
- A quarter-smile, asymmetric, lifting only the left side, that appears when he is about to deliver violence. Appears also, less often, when something genuinely amuses him; intimates have learned the difference.
- A complete facial slackening — affect drains, eyes go middle-distance, mouth parts perhaps three millimeters — that signals an imminent dissociative event. Lasts one to four seconds. The person who emerges may not be the same person.
- The Marlene-specific softening: when she enters his field of vision unannounced, the medial brow furrow releases for perhaps half a second before he reconstructs the guarded expression. This is one of the most reliable involuntary tells on his body.

**Eyes.** Brown, near-black under poor light. Tracks fast. Saccadic pattern is highly trained — on entering any space, the eyes execute a perimeter sweep (entrances, weapons-of-opportunity, civilians, threats) inside two seconds, without head movement. He has done this for so long that he cannot turn it off. In conversation he holds eye contact slightly longer than the social norm — an intimidation habit from interrogation work that he no longer means as intimidation but that everyone reads as such. Pupillary response to Khonshu's apparent presence: dilation that is *not* mood-congruent with ambient light, a fact a careful observer (e.g., a neurologist, Lemire-era) has remarked on.

**Smile.** Rare. The full smile — both sides of the mouth, eye-crinkle, teeth showing — is reserved for Gena's diner, Gena's sons, and intermittently Marlene at her most disarming. It transforms the face entirely and makes him look ten years younger; he seems to know this and rations it.

---

### 4. THE HANDS

The hands are their own dossier. In addition to the scarring noted above:

- **Constant low-level activity at rest.** Fingers of the dominant hand will *cycle* — thumb to index, thumb to middle, thumb to ring, thumb to little, in repeat — when he is thinking. Frequency increases under stress; ceases entirely under threat (the hand goes still and ready).
- **The crescent.** When seated and idle, the right index finger traces a small arc on whatever surface is to hand — a tabletop, the side of a coffee mug, his own thigh. Crescent-shaped. He is not aware of it. Marlene has watched him do it for forty years.
- **Coin-work.** Jake-state especially, but Marc as well: a single coin walked across the knuckles, or rolled between the fingers, when on stakeout or waiting. Right hand only. Tradecraft as soothing behavior.
- **Knuckle-cracking.** Each hand, in sequence, before any anticipated violence — finger by finger, then the wrists. It is partially ritual, partially genuine joint preparation (the old fractures stiffen). He has tried to stop. He has not stopped.
- **Reach pattern.** When handed an object, he takes it with the off-hand, keeping the dominant hand free. Universal across alters. A surveillance team would identify this within the first hour of observation.
- **Touch with intimates.** With Marlene, he initiates contact through the back of his fingers against her arm or cheek — knuckles first, not palm. The palm is for striking; the back of the hand is for tenderness. He learned this somewhere and has never deviated. With children he uses the full open palm to the top of the head, briefly, then withdraws.

---

### 5. VOICE AND BREATH

**Voice.** Baseline a low baritone, slightly gravelled — the gravel is partial vocal-cord scarring (intubation, *The Bottom* arc) layered over decades of yelling under masks. Speaks at lower volume than his frame suggests; people lean toward him to hear, which he uses. His register *drops* further under stress (the calm-voice of a man preparing to do something terrible), and *rises* slightly during alter-switches — Steven's voice sits perhaps a fourth higher and acquires a transatlantic crispness; Jake's voice is rougher, faster, with a Brooklyn-edged lower-class cadence that Marc-primary does not use.

**Speech rate.** Marc-primary speaks slowly, with pauses he does not feel obligated to fill. Steven speaks at conversational-business pace, with verbal fluency. Jake speaks fast, slang-dense, often clipping word endings. Cross-state contamination is a reliable diagnostic for incipient breakdown: when Marc-primary starts using Jake's clipped endings mid-sentence, or Steven loses the transatlantic polish, the architecture is destabilizing.

**Breath.** Trained diaphragmatic breathing — Marine-issued, boxer-reinforced. Resting respiratory rate is low (ten to twelve). Under threat he executes a long exhale before engagement — the tactical breath, twice as long out as in, hits the parasympathetic and steadies the hand. He breathes through the nose almost exclusively except in active exertion. The single most reliable tell that he is panicking (rare) is mouth-breathing in a non-exertional context.

**Silences.** He uses silence aggressively. Will let a question hang for a count of five, six, seven without flinching. Interrogators trained on him learn not to fill the gap; civilians never learn.

---

### 6. SLEEP ARCHITECTURE

Catastrophically disordered, longitudinally.

**Schedule.** Nominal sleep window 0500–1100, but observed compliance is poor. Total sleep time across a representative week: thirty to forty hours, fragmented into two to four blocks. Naps in safe houses, in vehicles, on Marlene's couch, in the back booth of Gena's diner. The Midnight Mission era introduces something closer to scheduled rest but the schedule is observed only by Steven; Marc and Jake violate it routinely.

**Onset.** Long. Twenty to ninety minutes of wakeful lying — hands behind head or one arm across the eyes, breathing controlled but not asleep. He does not read in bed; he does not watch screens; he lies in the dark and listens. Sleep onset is often facilitated by alcohol (problem-era) or by sheer exhaustion after a fight.

**Architecture.** Likely REM-fragmented, with frequent partial arousals. Lemire-era documentation of fugue during sleep transitions is consistent with disrupted NREM-to-REM cycling; one mechanism for the dissociative phenomena is precisely that the boundaries between sleep and waking, and between alters, share neurochemistry.

**Nightmares.** Recurrent, thematically constrained: the desert; the statue; the moment of dying; his father's face in distress. He does not cry out in nightmares (Marines trained that out); he sweats. Marlene has reported finding the sheets soaked. He wakes silently and is fully alert inside two seconds — a useful trait operationally, a terrible one for any partner who reaches for him in the dark. Multiple canonical instances of him reflexively gripping a wrist hard enough to bruise before recognizing the wrist's owner.

**Threshold behaviors.** Falls asleep faster after violence than after rest. Stays asleep longer in moonlight than in artificial light; will sometimes pull curtains open before sleeping. He believes this is Khonshu. The phenomenon is real regardless of attribution.

---

### 7. EATING AND HYDRATION

**Pattern.** Erratic at baseline; structured only when someone else is present to structure it. Marlene-era meals are regular and shared; solo-era meals are coffee, eggs at Gena's, protein bars in pockets, water from taps.

**Preferences.** Mediterranean and Levantine foods — old comfort. Strong black coffee, by the pot. Avoids pork (the Jewish identity, even at his most lapsed, retains this single line; Lemire confirms). Will eat anything if mission requires it. Sweet tooth, controlled but real — Gena's pie is a recurring weakness, and there is canonical evidence of him eating an entire slice with his back to the door, which he never otherwise does.

**Alcohol.** Whiskey when drinking — neat, sipped slowly during the controlled years, gulped during the Huston-era spiral. Cleaner periods are *abstinent* rather than moderated; he does not appear to have a moderate gear with alcohol.

**Cigarettes.** Inconsistent across eras. Smokes more during stakeout and surveillance; quits and restarts. The Jake alter is the heavier smoker. A pack of matches from a specific bar will live in his coat for years.

**Eating posture.** Sits with his back to a wall, ninety-five percent of observed meals. Eats fast — Marine pace, never broken. Fork in the dominant hand even for foods that would more efficiently use the other. Drinks water in large single gulps rather than sipping.

---

### 8. GROOMING AND DRESS

**Hair.** Black, going to grey at the temples in later eras; he does not dye it. Cut short — a length he can maintain himself with clippers, never trusted to a barber for more than three or four sessions before he switches shops. Beard growth is heavy; he is clean-shaven for operational identities and lets it grow into stubble in collapse. The decision to shave is itself diagnostic — a clean jaw the morning after a bad night means he has decided to keep functioning.

**Nails.** Short, clean, kept that way with a folding knife rather than clippers. Will trim them in the middle of a conversation without breaking eye contact.

**Bathing.** Showers hot — punishingly hot — and long. The shower is one of his only reliable private rituals. He does not sing. He stands under the water for ten to fifteen minutes before beginning to wash. The post-violence shower can run forty minutes.

**Scent.** Subject does not wear cologne. There is a faint, persistent smell on him of clean cotton, gun oil, and the particular Old World soap his housekeeping rotation prefers. The Steven identity occasionally wears something expensive and citrus. Jake smells of cigarettes and diner coffee.

**Wardrobe — civilian.** Dark colors, plain cuts, layers. Two-jacket habit: an outer for weather and concealment, an inner for movement. Belt always; wallet in the inside breast pocket, never the hip. Watch on the left wrist, analog, mechanical, wound by hand each morning — the winding is a small grounding ritual.

**Wardrobe — Steven.** Tailored. He knows the tailor by name and tips well. Cufflinks. Pocket square only on occasions that demand it; he does not enjoy them.

**Wardrobe — Jake.** A windbreaker, jeans, a cap. He looks like nobody. This is the point.

**Wardrobe — operational.** White, always white. The white is the entire thesis of his life made textile. He has explained, more than once and to more than one writer, that he wants to be seen. The cape is functional (concealment of weapons, breaking of silhouette, theatrical effect on targets) and confessional (the man underneath wants to be punished by someone who can see him clearly).

---

### 9. SEXUAL AND INTIMATE BEHAVIOR

Sparsely documented but coherent across what canon provides.

**Pattern.** Long-term, episodic, almost exclusively centered on Marlene. Brief involvements outside that orbit are characterized by emotional unavailability and abrupt withdrawal. He is not promiscuous. He is not asexual. He is *avoidant under intimacy pressure,* and sexual contact for him is an intimacy event he can rarely tolerate at sustained frequency.

**Physical presentation.** Slow to initiate, slow to disrobe — the scars and the body are a complicated text and he is aware of being read. He does not look in mirrors during. He keeps the lights low not for atmosphere but because he prefers to feel his way; the body memory of violence in bright light is too near.

**During intimacy.** Quiet. Watches her face more than is comfortable for either party. Hands deliberate, almost careful to a fault — the same back-of-the-hand approach scaled up. Cannot tolerate being held down even gently; one observed instance of Marlene pinning his wrists in play triggered a partial dissociative episode and a hard stop.

**After.** Often the most verbal he becomes in any context. The post-intimacy window is when he has, historically, said the truest things he says — to Marlene, to one or two others. The window closes within hours.

**Alter-state.** Steven Grant is a more confident lover by Marlene's account, more performative, more verbally appreciative — and Marlene has reported, with discomfort, knowing the difference and not always knowing which one she went to bed with. This is, more than any other single piece of evidence, the locus of the wound between them. Jake does not appear sexually with Marlene. Jake's intimate life, if any, is undocumented and probably deliberately so.

---

### 10. RITUALS, TICS, AND COMPULSIONS

A partial list of behaviors that recur across thirty years of observation:

- **The crescent-trace** with the right index finger (see hands, above). Frequency increases under cognitive load.
- **Knuckle-cracking sequence** before anticipated violence; finger by finger, then wrist rotation, total elapsed time about four seconds.
- **Perimeter sweep** on entering any room, executed within two seconds, eyes only.
- **Back-to-wall seating** in every interior space. Will rearrange furniture, or refuse a seat, to obtain it. He attributes this to tradecraft. It is also that he cannot tolerate unseen space behind him during dissociative-vulnerable moments.
- **Watch-winding** at the same time each morning — when he is sleeping at all.
- **Coin-walking** across the knuckles when waiting.
- **The moon-check.** When outdoors after dark, he glances up at the moon within the first ten seconds, every time. He does not appear to know he does this. Khonshu-attribution is obvious; the behavior predates, by his own admission in the Lemire run, the Khonshu encounter — he did it as a boy.
- **The shower.** As above. Long, hot, ritualized.
- **The pre-engagement breath.** Long exhale, twice the inhale, immediately before initiating combat. Sometimes audible.
- **The bedside weapon.** Always present. Position rotates — under the pillow, in the nightstand, on the floor within reach — but presence is invariant. He has injured Marlene reaching for it once. He keeps it anyway.
- **Refusal of the handshake-then-pat** (the secondary touch some men add). He does the handshake; he does not add the touch. Symmetrically, he flinches almost imperceptibly when others do it to him.
- **The double-take to the right-upper field of vision.** Khonshu's apparent perch. Frequency varies by era; high in Huston, low in Ellis, moderate in MacKay.
- **Touching the chest scar** absently, through clothing, during conversations about Sudan or Bushman. Right hand, three fingers, brief pressure. He does not know he does this either.

---

### 11. STATE-SHIFT CHOREOGRAPHY

The transition between alters has a physical signature that a trained observer learns. The full sequence, observed multiple times:

1. **Pre-switch stillness** — a beat of complete motor arrest, usually mid-sentence or mid-gesture.
2. **Facial slackening** — affect drains for one to four seconds.
3. **A single deeper breath** — the inhale is sharper than baseline.
4. **The blink flutter** — two to four rapid blinks.
5. **Postural reorganization** — shoulders rise or drop, chin lifts or sets, weight redistributes. Steven gains height; Jake loses it.
6. **Hand reset** — the dominant hand reorganizes its idle behavior. Marc's crescent-trace becomes Steven's open-palm gesture or Jake's pocket-jam.
7. **Voice change** — register, rate, accent, lexicon shift inside the first three words spoken.

Total elapsed time: approximately six to twelve seconds. Under stress, the sequence telescopes to two or three. Under sedation or in the asylum arcs, it stalls — the slackening occurs but the reorganization fails, leaving him affectless and slack-jawed, which is one of the most distressing presentations to those who know him.

The *reverse* transition — coming back to Marc-primary — is harder to read. It often happens during sleep


## Attachment & Relational Patterns

# UATU DOSSIER — MARC SPECTOR / MOON KNIGHT
## Section 6: Attachment & Relational Patterns

---

### 6.1 Attachment Classification and Its Origin

Subject presents a **disorganized-fearful attachment style with avoidant overlay**, of the kind reliably produced by a caregiving environment in which the available adult was simultaneously the source of comfort and the source of threat — or in which one parent provided love that could not protect and another provided contact that wounded. The original objects mapped onto Marc's developing template are:

- **Elias Spector (father, rabbi, Holocaust survivor):** loving, intellectually generous, religiously serious, *non-protective* in any physical sense. To a child organizing his nervous system around safety after the family transmission of the Shoah, paternal pacifism reads not as virtue but as defenselessness. Marc's early aggression toward Elias (documented by Moench in flashbacks and made central by Lemire) is not rebellion in the ordinary adolescent register; it is the panicked rage of a child who has assessed his protector and found him insufficient against the size of the world's evil. Love is filed under *insufficient*. From this, the lifelong axiom: **the people who love me cannot save me, so I must not allow saving from them to be the basis of bond.**
- **The mother (variable across continuities, but consistent in late retcons — Bemis, MacKay):** mentally ill, abusive, frightening; the secret of the house. Marc's coping is *split her off* — both within his memory (dissociated until adulthood) and within his developing internal model of woman/caregiver/love. From this, the second axiom: **the person who hurts me is also the person to whom I am most bound; I will keep loving her by not remembering her.**

The combination is the textbook substrate for disorganized attachment: approach and avoidance fire simultaneously, and the resolution the child finds is to **distribute the contradiction across multiple selves** rather than hold it in one. The dissociative architecture that becomes diagnostically central in adulthood begins here as a *relational* solution before it is a *traumatic* one. Steven can be loved without danger because Steven is not the wounded boy. Jake can be hated and feared without grief because Jake never had a mother. Marc retains the wound and absorbs the cost.

This produces a man whose default relational posture is **proximity-seeking with built-in escape velocity** — he draws people in close enough to know him, then triggers his own withdrawal before they can demand the integration he cannot perform.

---

### 6.2 Bonding: How Subject Forms Attachments

Subject bonds through **shared danger, shared damage, or service rendered** — never through ordinary social affiliation. His friendships are forged in fire and maintained by usefulness; he does not have a single canonical relationship that began at a dinner party. Mapped longitudinally:

- **Marlene Alraune:** met at the moment of her father's murder and his own near-death (MK vol.1 #1). The originating bond is *I failed to save what mattered to you and you nursed me back from death anyway* — a transaction of catastrophic mutual obligation, not romance. Every subsequent attempt at ordinary romance with Marlene fails because the relationship has no ordinary register to fall back on; stripped of crisis, it becomes an impossible ask.
- **Jean-Paul "Frenchie" DuChamp:** combat brother from the mercenary years. The bond is *we did the unspeakable together and only the other knows.* Frenchie's later coming out (Huston run) and Marc's unconditional acceptance is one of the few clean emotional events in the file — because it asked nothing of Marc's interior, only of his loyalty, which he gives easily. Loyalty is cheap for him; intimacy is expensive.
- **Gena Landers and her sons:** the diner-owner family from the Moench run. Bond formed through **Jake Lockley's** street persona — i.e., not through Marc-self at all. He can love this family because the alter who knows them holds the relationship; Marc-primary can visit it without owing it. Note the protective ferocity toward her sons: surrogate-paternal energy, expressed through an alter, at a safe distance.
- **Reese (MacKay run):** rescued vampire-survivor; bond formed through *I will keep you alive while you become whoever you are becoming.* Mentorship as attachment vector — safer than peerage.
- **Soldier (the dog, MacKay run):** load-bearing. The only relationship in the file with zero risk of integration-demand. He is visibly more openly tender with the dog than with any human. This is diagnostic, not comic relief.
- **Hunter's Moon / Dr. Badr (MacKay):** fellow avatar, fellow Jewish-coded servant of the same god — a peer who shares the *theological* frame without requiring the *psychological* one. Marc can be known by him in exactly one dimension, which is exactly the bandwidth Marc can sustain.

**The bonding signature:** he attaches by *being needed in a specific functional role*, and the bond persists only as long as the role does. He does not know how to be loved for being. He knows how to be loved for *doing.*

---

### 6.3 Distrust: How Subject Withholds and Watches

Subject's distrust is **structural, layered, and asymmetric** — he extends conditional trust generously at the operational level and almost never at the interior level. Observable patterns:

- **Compartmentation by alter.** Different people in his life know different selves. Marlene knows Marc and (reluctantly) Steven; Gena's family knows Jake; Avengers-tier peers know "Moon Knight" as a costume; psychiatrists know whichever self walked in. No single person holds the whole map. This is presented to others as discretion; it functions as **distributed deniability of self.** Even if one relationship betrays him, only one face is exposed.
- **Pre-emptive disclosure as defense.** "I'm crazy" delivered early in any encounter — to allies, to lovers, to therapists. This looks like vulnerability and functions as armor: by naming the wound first, he controls its valence and pre-empts any later revelation by another party. It is the verbal equivalent of the white costume — *I tell you what I am so you cannot find it out.*
- **Vetting through provocation.** He tests new allies by being unpleasant, erratic, or operationally reckless and watching how they metabolize it. Those who stay despite the provocation pass; those who try to fix him fail. The vetting protocol is unconscious but consistent across decades.
- **Institutional distrust, total.** CIA (which used him), Committee (which paid him), Avengers (which managed him), hospitals (which confined him), the NYPD (which periodically hunts him). Every institution in his life has either betrayed him or attempted to contain him. He treats organizational loyalty as a category error. The Midnight Mission is the only institution he trusts because he built it, runs it, and can dissolve it.
- **Surveillance reciprocity.** He runs intelligence on his own allies. Jake's network includes intel on Frenchie's movements, Marlene's residences, Gena's diner; Steven's financial apparatus tracks the holdings of anyone Marc Spector has ever owed money. He maintains this not from hostility but from *anticipatory grief* — he expects to be left and is mapping the topography of the future loss in advance.

---

### 6.4 Betrayal: How Subject Wounds and Is Wounded

**How he betrays:** rarely actively, almost always through **dissociative absence** — disappearing into an alter for weeks, missing the agreed-upon event because Jake had a case, failing to come home because Steven had a charity gala, going dark for a season because Marc collapsed. The betrayal is not infidelity or deceit in the ordinary sense; it is *unreliability of presence.* Marlene's accumulated grievance through every era of the title is some version of: *I never know which of you is going to be here, and sometimes none of you is.* He also betrays by **pre-emptive rupture** — sensing intimacy approaching a threshold he cannot hold, he picks the fight, accepts the mission, takes the wound, that drives the partner away. He calls this protecting them. It is partly that and largely an evacuation of his own panic.

**How he is wounded:** disproportionately by *being managed.* When allies coordinate behind his back to commit him, to intervene on his substance use, to "stage" his recovery, he reads it — accurately — as the recapitulation of his mother's instability being handled around him by adults who decided what reality he was allowed to inhabit. The Huston-era and Lemire-era responses to therapeutic intervention are not anti-treatment in principle; they are anti-*deception.* He will accept help offered directly. He will rage against help arranged covertly. Secondary wound vectors:

- Being told Khonshu is not real *while in a depleted state* (asylum arc): produces collapse, because the only stable scaffolding is being kicked out.
- Being told he is a *good man* by someone whose judgment he respects: produces a flinch, then an escalation of self-punishing behavior, because the praise indexes a debt he believes he cannot pay.
- Witnessing harm to a person under his protection: produces a guilt response so absolute that it can trigger alter-switching mid-event.
- Mercy from an enemy: humiliating in a way that combat injury is not, because it implies the enemy saw something in him worth sparing, which he cannot reconcile with his self-concept.

---

### 6.5 Repair: How Subject Returns

Repair, when it happens, follows a **ritualized, non-verbal, action-coded** script. He does not apologize in words well or often; the apology is delivered in gesture:

- *Re-appearance at the threshold.* After a fugue or disappearance, he simply shows up — at Marlene's door, at the diner, at Frenchie's hangar — and resumes as if continuous. The implicit ask is: *let the absence not need to be named.* Sometimes granted, often refused; the refusal is what ends the relationship phase.
- *Tactical gift.* A solved case, an enemy neutralized, a debt cleared, a building rebuilt. Money (Steven's funds) deployed silently. The gift is calibrated to the wound it is meant to address but never overtly connected to it.
- *Allowing himself to be cared for, briefly.* He will sit still and be bandaged, fed, slept beside, for one cycle — and then go. The brief acceptance of care *is* the apology; the leaving is the limit.
- *Naming the failure to a third party so it travels back.* He will confess to Frenchie what he could not confess to Marlene, knowing Frenchie will tell her. Triangulated repair — because direct repair is intolerable.

True repair, by which is meant durable resumption of relationship at full prior depth, has happened a vanishingly small number of times in his life. With Frenchie, repeatedly — because Frenchie has organized his own life around forgiving Marc without requiring change. With Marlene, partially and recurrently — each cycle a little shorter, each separation a little longer. With Khonshu, ritually and constantly — the god-relation is built entirely on rupture-and-return as its operating principle, which is why it is the most stable bond in the file.

---

### 6.6 Intimacy and Dependency

Subject's capacity for intimacy is **high in moment, low in duration.** He can be extraordinarily present — fully attuned, gentle, even tender — for an evening, a night, a crisis. He cannot sustain this presence across the ordinary register of weeks-and-months of partnered life because:

1. **Continuity of self is the price of continuity of intimacy**, and his self is non-continuous by design. To be the same person across Tuesday-Wednesday-Thursday for the lover requires him to suppress the alter-switching that is his affect-regulation apparatus, which produces decompensation.
2. **Intimacy invites being known whole**, which is the one thing he has organized his entire psychic architecture against. To be known whole is to be known as the mercenary, as the son who failed his father, as the boy who could not protect himself from his mother, as the avatar of a god who may or may not exist. The integration the lover wants is the catastrophe he survives by avoiding.
3. **Dependency, accepted, is dependency that can be withdrawn.** If he allows himself to need Marlene, then Marlene's death or departure becomes survivable only by another self-shattering. He has had enough of those. Better to organize the relationship such that the need is never fully placed.

His **dependency pattern** is therefore *displaced and ritualized.* He is profoundly dependent on Khonshu (a relation that cannot be lost in the ordinary way), heavily dependent on the alter-system (which is internal and portable), operationally dependent on Frenchie (a dependency dressed as partnership), and ambivalently dependent on Marlene (the one human dependency he half-admits, which is why she is the one figure who can destabilize him most). With everyone else — Avengers, clients, the Midnight Mission's wards — the dependency vector runs *toward him,* never from him. He is the helper. Being the helped requires a position he cannot occupy without panic.

Sexual intimacy follows the same pattern: he is, by all canonical implication, a generous and attentive partner in encounter and a catastrophic partner in continuance. Marlene's reports across decades suggest the early-relationship Marc is profoundly different from the cohabiting Marc — the former is courtship, which has a role; the latter is partnership, which requires a self.

---

### 6.7 The Relational Template, Mapped

Beneath the specific relationships is **one repeating template,** observable from the Moench origin material through the MacKay era and applicable to every meaningful figure in his life. The template runs in five phases:

**Phase 1 — Recognition through wound.** Subject meets the other under conditions of damage (theirs, his, or shared). He identifies in them either *a victim he can protect* or *a wounded operator he can serve alongside.* The relationship is encoded from the first contact as having a *functional* purpose. No purpose, no bond.

**Phase 2 — Service and devotion.** Subject overdelivers. He is generous with money, with time, with violence on the other's behalf, with his body. He is *easy* to love at this phase because he asks for nothing and gives extravagantly. The other often interprets this as the beginning of a deepening intimacy. It is in fact the *full extent* of the intimacy he can sustainably offer.

**Phase 3 — Approach to the integration threshold.** The other, encouraged by Phase 2, asks for more — for continuity, for interior access, for the whole man. Subject feels the pressure as an inward squeeze. Alter-switching increases. Sleep degrades. Khonshu's voice gets louder. Substance use, if available, recurs. The body starts to perform the refusal the mouth cannot.

**Phase 4 — Rupture, coded as something else.** Subject precipitates an exit. A mission cannot be refused. An old enemy resurfaces. A fugue lasts longer than usual. A fight is picked over an issue that is not the issue. He disappears.
