The other is left to interpret the rupture; the most common interpretation, that he does not love them, is the one he prefers them to hold, because it is less dangerous to him than the truth (that he loves them past his capacity to bear).

**Phase 5 — Return, or non-return.** If the other survives the rupture without demanding its naming, Phase 1 begins again at a slightly lower amplitude. If the other demands the rupture be processed, the relationship ends or downgrades to operational acquaintance. Marlene has cycled through this loop perhaps a dozen times across his published life. Frenchie has cycled through it without ever forcing Phase 5 — which is why he is the most durable human bond on file. Khonshu's relationship runs on a compressed version of this loop on roughly a monthly basis.

---

### 6.8 Specific Recurring Relational Tells

A surveillance file's worth of granular signals, longitudinally consistent:

- He says goodbye as if it is hello. Departures are minimized; he does not stand at thresholds.
- He arrives at the homes of intimates without warning and without knocking when he has a key, but never sleeps over more than two consecutive nights without an operational reason.
- He pays for things silently — Marlene's apartments, Gena's diner's roof repair, Frenchie's plane's engine work — and refuses acknowledgment, sometimes denying he did it.
- He remembers, with eidetic precision, the small operational details of an ally's life (medication schedules, gun preferences, building blueprints) and forgets birthdays.
- He gives gifts that are *useful* and *protective* — a better lock, a panic button, a vetted lawyer's contact — rather than gifts that are *sentimental.*
- He touches allies almost exclusively in the context of injury — bandaging, carrying, catching. Casual physical affection is rare and visibly difficult.
- In conversation, he positions himself with a sight line to the door and a hand within reach of a weapon, even with intimates in safe rooms. Marlene has stopped commenting on this; Frenchie never did.
- He uses different names for himself with different intimates, and tracks which name each is licensed to use. To be addressed by the wrong name by the wrong person produces a visible micro-startle.
- He grieves losses through *operational displacement* — the death of someone he loved produces an immediate case, a hunt, a mission. He does not sit shiva for himself; he hunts for himself. The MacKay run's reframing of the Midnight Mission as ministry is the first sustained attempt in his life to grieve through *building* rather than through *punishing,* and is the closest thing to integrative progress in the file.

---

### 6.9 Synthesis

Marc Spector loves a small number of people with a constancy disproportionate to his behavior, and his behavior is disproportionate because his architecture cannot hold the constancy without buckling. He has built, around the original disorganized attachment, a baroque secondary structure — alters, the god, the mission, the costume — that allows him to deliver the *substance* of love (protection, loyalty, service, presence-in-crisis) while withholding the *form* of love (continuity, integration, ordinary dependency, the shared interior). Those who have stayed in his life are those who have learned, painfully, to take what he can give in the modality he can give it. Those who tried to receive love from him in the modality they wanted have been ground down and have left.

He is, in the end, attached the way a man chained to a wall is attached: thoroughly, immovably, by an apparatus that also prevents him from walking forward into the relationship. The chain is the apparatus that has kept him alive. He knows it is the chain. He has, in fifty published years, never put down the key — because the moment he is free he will have to be one person, and he has never, in any era, in any writer's hands, been able to imagine surviving that.


## Defenses & Compensatory Mechanisms

# UATU DOSSIER — MARC SPECTOR / MOON KNIGHT
## Section: Defenses & Compensatory Mechanisms

---

### Preamble: How to Read This Architecture

The subject's defensive structure is not a stack; it is a *cathedral*. Each defense supports the next, and removing any single load-bearing element threatens collapse of the whole. The architecture has been under continuous construction since approximately age six (per Lemire flashback material), reinforced through adolescence (boxing → military), stress-tested in Sudan, and renovated repeatedly across every subsequent decompensation and remission cycle. Forty-eight years of observable behavior across the published record show *minimal* substitution of defenses — only modulation of their intensity and ordering. This is a fully mature defensive system in a fully mature ego, and the defenses must be respected as solutions before they are interrogated as pathology. The subject *would not have survived* without them. He still might not.

The ranking that follows moves from most primitive (Kernbergian psychotic-borderline level) to most mature (neurotic and adaptive). At any given moment the subject deploys defenses across the full vertical stack simultaneously; the trick of intervention is identifying which level is *load-bearing* in that hour.

---

### TIER I — PRIMITIVE / PSYCHOTIC-LEVEL DEFENSES

These are the foundation stones. They operate below conscious access. They are the defenses Marc was using before he could name them and before he met Khonshu.

#### 1. Dissociation (primary, structural)

The subject's master defense, around which everything else is organized. Manifests at multiple grain-sizes:

- **Macro-dissociation: alter formation.** Steven Grant, Jake Lockley, Marc Spector — and, in florid phases, additional borrowed identities (the hallucinated Avengers in the L.A. period; expanded rosters under Bemis; Mr. Knight as a contained suit-persona under Ellis). Each alter is a *functionally complete affect-and-skill bundle* designed to handle a class of situation Marc-primary cannot tolerate. Steven processes wealth, taste, and social standing — domains in which Marc the rabbi's-son-turned-mercenary feels he has no claim. Jake processes street violence, comic transgression, and the moral relief of being *low* rather than aspirational. Marc retains the depression, the guilt, the boxing-physical, the Khonshu line. Observable tells of an active switch: brief eye-flutter or downward gaze (~0.5–2s), shoulder reset, micro-realignment of stance, change in breath rate, accent shift (Steven's mid-Atlantic upper register; Jake's New York consonant-clipping; Marc's flatter Chicago baseline), and — across all eras — a change in dominant hand pressure on whatever object is held.
- **Meso-dissociation: state-switching without alter assumption.** Even in Marc-primary, observable shifts in affect-and-access. The man at the breakfast table is not the man at the rooftop edge ninety seconds later; the man interrogating a target is not the man calling Gena from a payphone afterward. These are not alter changes but *segmented Marc-states*, each with restricted access to the others' content.
- **Micro-dissociation: derealization in act.** Documented across the Huston run especially: scenes of extreme violence rendered with the subject reporting absence, fugue, or "watching myself." The carving of Bushman's face is the apex case. Marc executes the act with full motor competence and zero narratable interiority. Post-act, partial amnesia or screen-memory.
- **Sleep-transitional dissociation.** Insomnia broken by fugue episodes (Lemire #2–4); awakenings in unfamiliar locations; the alters as nightcrawlers while Marc-self sleeps.

Dissociation is what permits everything above it in the stack. Pull it and the patient does not become integrated; the patient becomes psychotic.

#### 2. Splitting

The world is sorted into pure-good and pure-evil bins with almost no mixed-object tolerance.

- **Pure-evil bin:** Bushman, Sun King, child-abusers, traffickers, the Committee, any antagonist who is structurally a mirror. License for unrestricted aggression. The bin's existence is *load-bearing* — without legible monsters, the violence has no container, and the subject has no purpose.
- **Pure-good bin:** Marlene (in idealized form), the helpless, children, fellow trauma survivors he has not yet had to disappoint. License for unconditional protection. The bin is also load-bearing — without sacred objects, the protection has no addressee.
- **Self in both bins, never one:** Marc as monster *or* Marc as instrument of God, never Marc-as-flawed-man. The white costume is a perfect splitting object: visually pure, deployed in service of bloody work.

Operational consequence: the subject cannot do *gradient* harm-reduction. He can kill a predator or rescue a child; he cannot mediate a custody dispute. Cases that cannot be split cannot be worked, and he refuses them or hands them to allies.

#### 3. Projective Identification

He puts disowned content into others and then acts on it as if it lived there. Most visible with:

- **Khonshu himself.** Marc's appetite for vengeance, his bloodlust, his refusal to retire — all attributable to "the god." Khonshu then *demands* what Marc wants, and Marc obeys what he himself sourced. This is projective identification scaled to theology.
- **Targets.** Antagonists are made to carry Marc's split-off self-contempt; their punishment is the punishment Marc cannot inflict on himself directly without dying.
- **Allies.** Marlene is made to carry his disowned wish for ordinary life. He then resents her for wanting it, leaves her for wanting it, returns to her because *he* wants it but cannot own it.

#### 4. Primitive Idealization and Devaluation

Khonshu is omnipotent when needed and a liar when convenient. Marlene is salvation and prison. Frenchie is the only man he trusts and a man he leaves out of every important decision. The Avengers are colleagues and contemptible amateurs. The institutional psychiatry that holds him is rescue and persecution. Oscillation occurs over hours, not weeks; the prior valence is genuinely *not retrievable* during the current one.

#### 5. Somatization and Conversion

The body carries what the mind will not. Chronic pain disproportionate to current injury; somatic flare-ups timed to anniversaries of Sudan; tension headaches during periods of forced inactivity; the post-Bushman paralysis episode (Huston) reads in part as conversion — neurological exam findings inconsistent with imaging, mobility returning at the precise moment Khonshu's voice resumes. The body is the only honest reporter of an affect the mind has dissociated.

---

### TIER II — IMMATURE / BORDERLINE-LEVEL DEFENSES

These are the working defenses of daily operation — the ones a trained observer sees first.

#### 6. Identification with the Aggressor

The boy who could not be Elias because Elias was defenseless became the boxer, the Marine, the mercenary. The mercenary who served Bushman became, after Sudan, the *avenger* who killed Bushman in Bushman's own register — disproportionate, ritualized, face-marking violence. The face-carving is the diagnostic event: it is *Bushman's* signature inflicted on Bushman, and later (Huston) *worn* by Marc. He does not just defeat the aggressor; he becomes him in order to defeat him, and the becoming sticks.

Operational legacy: every subsequent enemy is met first with *their* methods, then with Marc's. This is why he is so effective against asymmetric opponents — he learns their grammar instinctively because identification-with-the-aggressor is his lifelong cognitive habit. It is also why prolonged contact with an enemy leaves residue: he absorbs them.

#### 7. Reaction Formation

The defensive turn that defines the *shape* of his life. Each successive identity is the negation of the prior:

- Rabbi's son → boxer (gentleness → controlled violence)
- Boxer → Marine (private violence → sanctioned violence)
- Marine → CIA → mercenary (sanctioned → unsanctioned violence for pay)
- Mercenary → avenger (violence for pay → violence as expiation)
- Avenger → pastor of the broken (violence as expiation → witnessing of the wounded)

Each move *opposes* the prior identity rather than integrating it; each leaves the prior unmetabolized and available for return under stress. He is not a synthesis; he is a stack of negations.

The white costume is reaction formation in textile: the man who has done darkness clothed in the maximum-visibility opposite. He has said in canon he wants criminals to see him coming. This is reaction formation made tactical.

#### 8. Turning Passive into Active

He was beaten unconscious and left for dead in a desert. He has, every night since, sought out beatings and near-deaths. The repetition is not compulsive in a freudian-blind sense; it is *engineered*. He chooses the rooftop, the odds, the proximity to the blade. By administering his own near-death repeatedly, he refuses to be the man who lay passively in the sand waiting for Khonshu's statue to do something. The Sudan moment is rewritten in every rooftop landing.

Tell: a recurring micro-behavior across all writers of *moving toward* incoming force in the last 200ms of an engagement when retreat would be equally available. He closes distance on knives. He does not flinch in the directions an uninjured man flinches.

#### 9. Acting Out

Affect that cannot be contained is discharged into behavior. Specifically:

- Grief discharged as patrol — Marlene's near-deaths and departures invariably followed by escalations in nightly violence.
- Rage discharged into target selection — periods of high Khonshu pressure correlate with hunts of escalating brutality (the Bottom-era killing-spree against the Committee remnants).
- Despair discharged as risk — the deeper the depression, the more reckless the engagement profile.

He almost never *says* the feeling. The feeling becomes the night's work.

#### 10. Devaluation of Self

A sustained, organized contempt for his own person used as defense against expecting better of himself and being disappointed. "I'm not a good man" is preemptive — said *to* allies so that allies cannot accuse him of it later. This is also weaponized self-knowledge (see Negative Compensations below).

#### 11. Magical Thinking / Theological Apophenia

Pattern-recognition pushed past the data: the Khonshu frame reads every coincidence as the god's hand. This is defensive because it ensures *nothing is random* — randomness is the deepest threat to a dissociative system, because randomness means events are not for him and his suffering has no narrative. The crescent appears in moonlight on a puddle and he reads it as instruction. He is rarely wrong in tactically useful ways (apophenia in a hyper-vigilant operator yields high false-positive rates that nonetheless catch real signal), which reinforces the defense.

#### 12. Counter-Dependence

He will not need. He will be needed. The asymmetry is enforced violently. He gives without receiving because receiving threatens the architecture — to receive is to be vulnerable is to be Elias is to be killable. Frenchie has spent forty-plus published years caring for a man who has never let himself be cared for in return without immediate retaliation by way of distance, danger, or disappearance.

#### 13. Omnipotent Control (alternating with Helpless Surrender)

He oscillates between *I will save everyone in this building tonight* and *I am Khonshu's slave and have no will of my own*. Both poles refuse the middle ground of bounded agency, which is the only ground from which sustainable work is done. The Midnight Mission (MacKay) is the first observable structure that *forces* him to operate in the middle — accept a case, work it within limits, decline cases outside scope. It is the most adaptive structure of his life and he resists it weekly.

---

### TIER III — NEUROTIC-LEVEL DEFENSES

The defenses of his higher-functioning periods. Present throughout but dominant in Ellis and MacKay eras.

#### 14. Intellectualization

He talks about his condition in clinical register to keep it at arm's length. He uses the word *alters*. He uses the word *dissociation*. He has read about himself. The vocabulary is correct and the vocabulary is also armor — naming the thing in DSM language is a way of holding it at a distance from the felt sense of it. Lemire's asylum arc weaponizes this against him: the psychiatrist uses Marc's own intellectualized vocabulary to dissolve Marc's mission.

#### 15. Isolation of Affect

He can describe Sudan factually — the temperature, the layout of the dig, the sequence of Bushman's blows, the distance to the statue — without affective accompaniment. The affect lives elsewhere (somatized, dissociated, projected) and is unavailable to the narrative voice. This is what permits him to brief allies and work cases involving content that *should* destabilize him.

#### 16. Rationalization

Every kill has a brief, deliverable justification. Every relapse has a context. Every abandonment of Marlene has a strategic frame ("she's safer without me"). The rationalizations are often partially true, which is what makes them durable defenses rather than transparent excuses.

#### 17. Displacement

Rage at Elias, at the absent/cruel mother, at Bushman, at himself — discharged onto the night's targets. Displacement is *why the work is effective*: the energy available for a given engagement vastly exceeds what the engagement alone could mobilize, because he is also fighting people who are not present.

#### 18. Reaction-Formation at the Neurotic Level

Beyond the structural negations above: tenderness in specific small acts toward children and victims that is the *exact opposite* of the brutality he has just dispensed two rooms away. Diapering an infant in a safe house in the same hour he scalped a trafficker. The tenderness is genuine *and* it is defending against the meaning of the brutality.

---

### TIER IV — MATURE / ADAPTIVE DEFENSES (Positive Compensatory Mechanisms)

These are the defenses that, if cultivated, constitute his actual treatment plan. They are present but under-deployed; every successful arc in his published life is a period of their ascendance.

#### 19. Sublimation

The cathedral's only true window. Channeling the fragmentation into casework, the violence into protection, the dissociative skill-bundles into a *team of one*. The Midnight Mission is the most mature form — running a clinic-of-sorts in which his pathology is the qualification. Hunter's Moon as a contrasting sane avatar foregrounds what sublimation looks like when it does not require fracture, which is both a hope and a wound for Marc.

#### 20. Altruism

Genuine, observable, and not reducible to defense — though it does defensive work. The protection of children is non-negotiable and pre-tactical; he will burn the operation to save the child. Care for traumatized victims after the fact (driving them home, finding them shelter, returning later to check) is documented across Moench, Huston, and MacKay runs. The altruism is what *earns* the small chosen family their loyalty and what permits Gena's diner to remain the only stable address in his life.

#### 21. Humor

Underrated in him. Jake's gallows wit is a defense (acting-out at the verbal level), but Marc-primary's dryness (Ellis, MacKay) is mature humor — the rueful self-observation of a man who has noticed his own absurdity and elected not to be destroyed by it. The jokes are aimed inward more than outward, which is the diagnostic of mature humor.

#### 22. Anticipation

He is a *planner*. Safe houses, cached weapons, escape routes, fallback identities — operational anticipation is constant. Emotional anticipation is rarer but present: he sees Marlene's departures coming and pre-grieves them; he sees his own decompensations coming and warns allies. The emotional anticipation is the seed of integration.

#### 23. Suppression (not repression)

He can, when needed, *consciously set aside* an affect to complete a task and return to the affect later. This is rare in DID profiles — most dissociative patients cannot suppress because dissociation has obviated the skill — and it speaks to a high baseline ego strength under the fracture. Ellis-era Marc shows this best: the suited operator who has parked his pathology in another room and will retrieve it after hours.

#### 24. Ritual / Liturgy as Containment

Crescent darts, the donning of the cowl, the patrol route, the call-sign to Frenchie, the visit to Gena's, the prayer he sometimes says in Hebrew despite the Egyptian iconography. Ritual is a mature defense when it contains rather than compels. For Marc the ritualism is *both*: liturgical when it bounds the night, compulsive when it cannot be skipped without panic. The work of his late period is moving more of his ritualism from compulsive to liturgical.

#### 25. Mentorship and Witness

Late-period sublimation: the use of his hard-earned knowledge of fragmentation to *recognize* and *companion* other fragmented people. Reese, the Mission's clients, the supernatural-afflicted. This is the closest thing to integration he has achieved: not becoming one, but offering his many to the service of others' many.

---

### NEGATIVE COMPENSATORY MECHANISMS (Failure Modes of the Architecture)

The same architecture, under load, produces predictable malfunctions.

- **Weaponized self-knowledge.** "I'm crazy, don't expect anything of me" deployed to preempt accountability and foreclose change. The diagnosis becomes a shield against the work the diagnosis implies.
- **Martyrdom-seeking dressed as courage.** The risk profile of his engagements consistently exceeds tactical necessity by a margin large enough to be its own signal. He is not reckless; he is *seeking the wound* and calling it duty.
- **Substance use as affect-regulation patch.** Alcohol and opioid analgesics (Huston explicit; relapses implied) when the alters cannot be summoned to do the regulatory work. The pattern: medical pain → opioid → opioid-mediated quieting of Khonshu → relief → dependence → withdrawal → louder Khonshu → escalation.
- **Compulsive identity-shedding.** When current configuration becomes intolerable, *change costume rather than change self.* Mr. Knight suit, Fist of Khonshu armor, Midnight Mission garb — wardrobe as defense against integration.
- **Geographical flight.** Chicago → military → Africa → New York → L.A. → New York → desert → New York. Movement as defense; new city as new self.
- **Sabotage of intimacy at threshold.** Reproducible behavior: when Marlene (or anyone) crosses a closeness threshold, he produces a crisis (a mission, a relapse, a disappearance) that re-establishes distance. He does this in the hours after the closeness is achieved, not days later.
- **Borrowed authority.** The L.A. hallucinated-Avengers period is the extreme case: he cannot authorize his own heroism, so he hallucinates Steve Rogers' voice to authorize it. Lower-grade across his career: invocation of Khonshu's mandate, of legal precedent he has not actually checked, of allies' implicit consent.
- **Pre-emptive contempt.** Devaluing institutions, peers, and helpers *before* they can devalue him. Most visible in Avengers tenure friction.
- **Iatrogenic loops with psychiatry.** Each hospitalization produces an alter-suppression that he experiences as identity-theft, which produces flight, which produces decompensation, which produces re-hospitalization. The system designed to help him is *consumed* by his architecture.
- **The cape itself as defense against the man.** The most uncomfortable item. Moon Knight protects the world *and* he protects Marc from having to be Marc. Any treatment plan that does not contend with the cape's defensive function will fail; any plan that removes it without replacement will kill him.

---

### Operational Note for Field Use

The architecture is *not* to be dismantled. It is to be *recruited*. Every successful period of the subject's life — Ellis's contained casework, MacKay's Mission — has worked by giving the defenses a *better job* rather than asking them to retire. Dissociation becomes division of labor. Splitting becomes case-triage. Identification with the aggressor becomes tactical empathy. Reaction formation becomes vocation. Turning passive into active becomes patrol. Sublimation becomes ministry.

Any approach — therapeutic, allied, or adversarial — that attempts to attack the defenses *as pathology* will trigger the entire stack downward into Tier I, with predictable consequences: dissociative collapse, projective combat, somatic crisis, and the summoning of Khonshu in his most punitive register. Any approach that *enlists* the defenses as the operational system they have become will find a colleague.

The cathedral stands. Walk in carefully. Do not touch the load-bearing stones.


## Longitudinal Psychological Profile

# UATU DOSSIER — SECTION 7: LONGITUDINAL PSYCHOLOGICAL PROFILE

*Decade-by-decade clinical mapping of affect regulation, cognitive style, self-concept, defensive architecture, and relational template across the subject's full documented lifespan (c. childhood Chicago through present-tense Midnight Mission operations). All inferences derived from cited behavioral record. Frameworks invoked: structural dissociation (van der Hart/Nijenhuis/Steele), polyvagal staging (Porges), object-relations splitting (Klein/Kernberg), C-PTSD (Herman/ICD-11), moral injury (Litz/Shay), attachment theory (Bowlby/Main), and traumatic neurocognitive sequelae.*

---

## I. CHILDHOOD AND LATE LATENCY (approx. ages 4–12) — *The Foundational Fracture*

**Affect regulation.** Already failing. The Lemire/Smallwood flashbacks (vol. 8 #5–8) and Bemis/Burrows asylum sequences depict a boy whose baseline arousal sits in the high sympathetic register — restless, easily roused to motor discharge, poor capacity for self-soothing. There is no observed evidence of a regulating dyadic partner: father Elias is structurally available but affectively miscalibrated for the child's threat-system needs (offers prayer, Torah, gentleness — modalities that require a regulated nervous system to receive); mother Wendy, in the MacKay-era retcon and Bemis allusions, is the *de*regulating presence — unpredictable, possibly cycling through her own affective illness, with cruelty episodes the boy could not metabolize. Affect is therefore managed *spatially*: he leaves rooms, runs, hits, and (the diagnostic kernel) **splits the self that has to be in the room with her from the self that loves the father**. Structural dissociation, in van der Hart's terms, begins here — the formation of an Apparently Normal Part that goes to school and an Emotional Part that holds maternal terror.

**Cognitive style.** Bright and pattern-seeking from the outset (the financial-acumen, tactical-planning, linguistic-aptitude evidence in adulthood implies a high baseline g; nothing in the developmental record suggests acquired retardation). But cognition is already conscripted to threat-detection: the Lemire flashbacks show the child Marc scanning the mother's face, the room, the door. Hypervigilance precedes trauma-naming. Imaginal capacity is robust and is doing double duty as defense — the boy who will later host Steven Grant and Jake Lockley is *already practicing* by populating his interior with companions, characters, voices. This is normal childhood imagination conscripted into proto-dissociative service; the architecture is being laid before it carries weight.

**Self-concept.** Inchoate but already negatively valenced. The implicit message of the maternal relationship — *something about me makes her do this* — sets the toxic core. The compensatory message from the father — *you are a soul, you are loved by Hashem* — does not land, because to accept it would require accepting the father as a reliable witness, and the father has been demonstrably unable to *stop* the mother. The boy's solution is to reject the father's frame entirely. He cannot be the father's beloved son in a house where the father is helpless; the identity is non-viable. He becomes, instead, the boy who *will not be helpless* — a pre-verbal vow that organizes the next sixty years.

**Defensive baseline by end of latency:** dissociation (primary), magical thinking (transitional), identification with the aggressor (proto), reaction formation (against father), motor discharge (running, fighting). The two pillars of the adult structure — *I will be the one who hits, not the one who is hit*, and *I will distribute the unbearable across several me's* — are both load-bearing by age twelve.

---

## II. ADOLESCENCE AND EARLY ADULTHOOD (ages ~13–22): BOXING, ESTRANGEMENT, ENLISTMENT — *The Body as Instrument*

**Affect regulation.** Outsourced to the body and to ritualized violence. Boxing is therapeutic in the crudest sense: it produces a *containing structure* (rounds, bells, rules, a corner man) within which his unmanageable sympathetic load can discharge and his parasympathetic system can recover, repeatedly. The ring is the first environment in his life that *fits* his nervous system. Sleep improves on training days; eating becomes regular; affect becomes legible to him for the first time, because it has a place to go. This is the developmentally critical fact: **Marc Spector learned, between thirteen and seventeen, that he is well only when he is being hit and hitting back in a sanctioned frame.** Every subsequent operational choice — Marines, mercenary, cape — is a search for that frame's continuation.

**Cognitive style.** Concretizes and tacticizes. Abstract/religious thought (the father's domain) is jettisoned with prejudice; pragmatic, embodied, situational cognition takes over. He is good at reading rooms, opponents, ground, weapons. School performance is presumed unremarkable — there is no evidence either way — but the kind of intelligence that will later run a multi-million-dollar Steven Grant portfolio is visibly being cultivated as *fight IQ* in this period.

**Self-concept.** Beginning to stabilize around a *negative-identity* organization (Erikson): he knows what he is *not* (not a rabbi's son, not a scholar, not a pacifist, not a victim) far better than what he is. The first explicit self-label is probably "fighter," then "soldier." Both are externally validated, which matters: the boy who could not get his mother's approval is now getting it from coaches, sergeants, paymasters. The self-concept is *contingent on performance under violence*, and is therefore structurally precarious — strip the performance, strip the self.

**Relational pattern.** Estranges from father (the canonical break with Elias, foregrounded by Lemire and MacKay), which is experienced as liberation but is psychodynamically a *re-enactment of the maternal abandonment in reverse*: he leaves before he can be left. Forms shallow same-sex affiliative bonds (training partners, fellow Marines) that are functional, replaceable, non-intimate. No documented serious romantic attachment in this period — Marlene is years away. The relational template is set: *peers in shared mission, no intimates*.

**Emergent pathology.** First combat exposure (Marines, presumed Lebanon/Beirut era given publication chronology) produces baseline PTSD symptomatology that he does not name as such. Nightmares, hyperarousal, intrusive imagery — all attributed by him to "the work" and managed by staying in the work. The dissociative architecture from childhood is now *adaptively useful* in combat; what was a developmental wound is now a battlefield asset. This is the perverse equilibrium that will define his thirties.

---

## III. THE MERCENARY YEARS (ages ~22–30): CIA, FREELANCE, BUSHMAN — *Moral Injury as Vocation*

**Affect regulation.** Increasingly chemical and increasingly distal. Alcohol enters the record as a normalized after-action ritual. Sleep is fragmented around contracts. The dissociative capacity that served combat is now operating in peacetime gaps — he loses time between jobs, drifts between cities, wakes in hotel rooms without full continuity. The brother Randall material (Moench original, contested by later retcons) belongs here in any reading: whether Randall was real or a dissociated externalization, the *function* of the Randall narrative is identical — Marc needed a container for the version of himself that killed for money without flinching, and Randall (real or hallucinated) carried it.

**Cognitive style.** Operationally peak; ethically narcotized. This is the period in which his tactical and HUMINT capacities reach professional ceiling — the skill base that will later distribute across Marc/Steven/Jake is consolidated here as a single, brutally competent mercenary cognition. Moral reasoning is bracketed: contracts are taken on contract logic, not ethical logic. This is not antisocial absence of conscience (the conscience is intact, as the eventual rupture proves); it is **moral injury in slow accumulation** (Litz/Shay), the quiet incremental violation of his own values, each one rationalized, each one depositing in an account that will be called in at the Temple of Khonshu.

**Self-concept.** Self-loathing crystallizes in this period but remains *unprocessable*. He cannot face it directly because facing it would require either suicide or career change, neither available. Instead, the self-concept bifurcates: the *operational* self is competent, valued, paid; the *moral* self is silenced, alcoholized, deferred. The phrase he will later repeat — "*I'm not a good man*" — is being earned, sentence by sentence, contract by contract, throughout this decade.

**Relational pattern.** Transactional in the extreme. The Bushman relationship is the diagnostic centerpiece: Marc accepts a charismatic, sadistic, capricious master and stays past every red flag. Read through attachment theory, Bushman is the *return of the mother* — unpredictable, dangerous, demanding, and impossible to leave because leaving has never been a regulated option for Marc's nervous system. He stays until Bushman commits an atrocity against the *unmistakably helpless* (the Alraune dig, with Marlene present), at which point the dissociated moral self breaks through the operational seal and forces the rupture. The rupture costs him his life. This is not coincidence; it is structure. He could only break with the bad object by dying.

---

## IV. THE TEMPLE AND THE FIRST DECADE OF THE CAPE (ages ~30–40): MOENCH-ERA OPERATIONS — *The Dissociation Goes Theological*

**Affect regulation.** Reorganized around a *sanctioning voice*. Whether Khonshu is metaphysically real or a dissociated persecutor/protector introject (the literature on DID describes such figures precisely), the *clinical function* is unmistakable: the voice gives orders, the orders structure the night, the night discharges the affect, the day permits collapse. For roughly a decade Marc achieves something like steady-state — not health, but **homeostatic pathology**. Marlene's presence supplies a parasympathetic anchor on the relational side; Frenchie supplies the operational corner-man function that boxing once provided. The system works.

**Cognitive style.** Tradecraft-organized, multi-modal, performatively flexible. The Steven Grant and Jake Lockley identities, in the Moench framing, are *deliberate covers* — but the writing already shows leakage (Marlene's repeated observation that he is "getting lost in them"). Diagnostically, this is the period in which what were dissociated *parts* in childhood become dissociated *identities* with sustained behavioral coherence — the structural shift from secondary to tertiary structural dissociation (van der Hart's terminology), accelerated by the Khonshu event functioning as a consolidating peri-traumatic ritual. Each alter takes a slice of cognitive style: Steven holds abstract/financial/social cognition (the father's intellectualism, finally usable because rebranded); Jake holds embodied/streetwise/aggressive cognition (the mercenary, retained but contained); Marc holds tactical/military/moral cognition (the operator with the cape). The distribution is *not redundant*; it is a remarkable functional adaptation that lets one nervous system run three operational profiles without any one of them collapsing from overload.

**Self-concept.** Officially: *I am Khonshu's Fist; I exist to punish those who prey on travelers in the night.* Privately: still the man who killed for money. The cape is parole, not pardon — he is doing time, indefinitely, in white. This is the period in which the **martyrdom-seeking** behavioral signature emerges most clearly: he takes hits he could slip, walks into traps he could outflank, accepts wounds as payment. The risk-taking reads to outsiders as courage and to clinical eyes as **chronic suicidality in vocational drag**.

**Relational pattern.** Marlene cohabitation; Frenchie deep operational bond; Gena and her sons (the diner family) as a chosen extended kinship. He is *capable of love in this period* — the Moench run is the warmest he will ever be on the page — but he cannot tolerate sustained intimacy with Marlene without dissociative withdrawal. The pattern is: closeness → switch (often to Steven, who can perform intimacy without feeling it) → Marlene experiences the switch → distance → reconciliation → repeat. This is the relational signature that will recur, unbroken, for the next forty years.

---

## V. THE LATE MOENCH/FIST-OF-KHONSHU AND DIXON-HAMA-PLATT YEARS (ages ~40–45): ACTION-HERO REMISSION — *Apparent Function, Suppressed Symptom*

**Affect regulation.** Looks better than it is. Operating in team contexts (West Coast Avengers, Secret Defenders) imposes external structure that absorbs symptom load; the visible Marc of this period is competent, sardonic, capable of comradeship. But this is the *functional remission* of a chronic illness in a supportive environment, not recovery. Dissociative switching is reduced because the operational frame is so dense it leaves no idle time for fracture to surface. Affect is *frozen rather than regulated* — narrow band, mission-locked.

**Cognitive style.** Tactical primacy; Steven and Jake recede in salience because their domains are less needed when the work is overt costumed combat. This is the period of greatest operational integration *at the cost of psychological depth*. He is least dissociated when least introspective — a finding consistent with DID literature, in which the apparent reduction of switching during high-structure periods is not integration but suppression.

**Self-concept.** Stabilizes around *vigilante professional*. The mercenary years are bracketed in the past tense; he speaks of himself as one who has crossed over. This is the most narratively coherent self-account of his life, and it is *partly defensive* — the coherence is purchased by not looking too closely. The Khonshu voice is quieter in this period because the operational frame is doing Khonshu's regulating work without needing the metaphysical interface.

**Relational pattern.** Marlene present but increasingly peripheral; the Avengers peers are tolerated but not absorbed. He notices that he does not feel like them and does not let them see why. Loyalty without intimacy, mission without disclosure — the relational profile of a man managing a secret illness inside a costume team.

---

## VI. THE HUSTON REWRITE / BOTTOM (ages ~45–48): COLLAPSE — *The Suppression Fails*

**Affect regulation.** Catastrophic decompensation. Bushman's crippling injury removes the operational frame; without nightly violence to discharge his autonomic load, the chronic-PTSD physiology surfaces unmediated. Alcohol and opioid analgesia substitute for the discharge function and produce predictable consequences: depressive deepening, cognitive blunting, somatic atrophy, social withdrawal. The Khonshu voice grows *louder* in this period, not quieter — consistent with the clinical pattern in which dissociative introjects intensify when the host is depleted and the alters cannot adequately hold the load. Marlene leaves. Frenchie leaves (with grievance). The chosen-family scaffolding collapses simultaneously with the operational scaffolding.

**Cognitive style.** Ruminative, paranoid-tinged, increasingly concrete. The flexible multi-modal cognition of the Moench years is degraded; he thinks in loops, in old grievances, in scenes from Sudan. **This is the period in which cumulative TBI most plausibly begins to express clinically** — the substrate damage from boxing, combat, mercenary work, and cape-era beatings, masked while operational, surfaces when the discharge stops.

**Self-concept.** Naked self-loathing, undefended. He sees himself accurately for perhaps the first time and cannot tolerate the seeing. The scalping/face-carving of Bushman, when he returns to the field, is the diagnostic event of the era: it is not punishment of Bushman (Bushman is already neutralized); it is **a ritualized confession of what Marc is**, performed on a proxy and worn as evidence. He returns to operations not redeemed but *reclassified* — he stops pretending he is a hero and accepts he is a weapon.

**Relational pattern.** Severed. He has to rebuild from rubble across the Huston arc, and the relationships he rebuilds (Marlene tentatively, Frenchie with permanent damage) are explicitly conditional and explicitly grieving. The fantasy of normal-cohabiting-Marlene is officially over; he will not pretend to it again.

---

## VII. THE BENDIS / LOS ANGELES INTERVAL (late 40s): FLORID DISSOCIATION — *Borrowed Authority*

**Affect regulation.** Outsourced to *hallucinated peers*. The Captain America / Wolverine / Spider-Man alters are the most diagnostically florid phase of his life and the most psychologically legible: unable to authorize his own heroism (because his self-concept will not bear the weight), he conjures the authority of figures who are *culturally licensed* to be heroes and lets them validate the next act of violence. This is dissociative use of *introjected cultural superegos* as a regulation mechanism. The fact that he picked those three — moral authority, feral instinct, everyman conscience — is itself a self-portrait of what he feels he lacks.

**Cognitive style.** Increasingly delusional in the *non-technical* sense: pattern-seeking has tipped into apophenia, narrative integration has tipped into confabulation, and he cannot reliably distinguish operational reasoning from grandiose self-mythology. Yet within this disorganization the *tactical* cognition still works — he completes operations. The dissociation is preserving function at the cost of reality-testing.

**Self-concept.** Fragmented to the point of incoherence. He cannot answer the question *who are you* without selecting a sub-self to answer. This is the lowest integration ebb of his documented life.

**Relational pattern.** Isolation with hallucinated company. The Bendis-era Marc is functionally alone, which his nervous system cannot tolerate, and the hallucinated alters are the company it generates. Real-relational impoverishment + dissociative richness — the inverse of health.

---

## VIII. THE ELLIS/SHALVEY "MR. KNIGHT" INTERVAL (late 40s to ~50): CONTAINMENT — *The Suited Remission*

**Affect regulation.** Improves markedly via *operational restriction*. The case-of-the-week structure, the suit as alternative uniform, the consulting-detective frame — these impose narrow channels on his violence and his attention. He sleeps better. He eats. Khonshu recedes. The alters are *deployed as tools* rather than experienced as invasions. This is the closest he comes, mid-life, to what would clinically be called *functional stabilization without integration* — the parts are cooperating without merging.

**Cognitive style.** Crisp, deductive, professional. The Steven-cognition and the Marc-tactical-cognition are running in parallel without conflict; he is using his full cognitive bandwidth without internal turbulence. This is the version of Marc most recognizable to outside observers as *high-functioning*.

**Self-concept.** Provisional, modest, work-oriented. He has stopped trying to answer *what am I* and is answering *what is the next case*. The reduction in existential load is therapeutic.

**Relational pattern.** Continued isolation but with *professional* contacts (police liaisons, clients) — a step up from the hallucinated peers of the Bendis interval. Still no intimate.

---

## IX. THE LEMIRE ASYLUM ARC (~age 50): EPISTEMOLOGICAL COLLAPSE — *The Diagnosis as Crisis*

**Affect regulation.** Catastrophic in the asylum sequences, then *re-stabilizing* through the unique route of accepting the dissociative architecture as identity rather than fighting it. The arc's narrative trick — that we cannot tell whether Khonshu is real or pure delusion — is *clinically* the experience of every DID patient confronted with a unifying psychiatric explanation: the offered integration would require dismantling the very system that has kept them alive. Marc's resistance to the asylum's narrative is not denial; it is **structural survival instinct**.

**Cognitive style.** Reality-testing acutely impaired by design (his own and the antagonist's); but at the meta-level he is doing the most sophisticated cognitive work of his life — interrogating the validity of his perceptions, his memories, his alters, his god. This is the first period in which he treats his own mind as an object of inquiry rather than a tool. Painful but developmentally significant.

**Self-concept.** Fundamentally revised. He emerges from this arc *knowing he is ill*, in a way the prior decades' "I'm not a good man" framing did not capture. The phrasing shifts from moral self-condemnation to clinical self-recognition. He stops asking *am I a monster* and starts asking *what am I, and how do I live with it*. This is the precondition for the MacKay-era ministry.

**Relational pattern.** Re-encounter with the alters as *interlocutors* rather than just inhabitants — the beginning of internal dialogue rather than internal warfare.

---

## X. THE BEMIS INTERVAL AND THE SUN KING (~age 51): MIRROR-CONFRONTATION

**Affect regulation.** Volatile, but with a new feature: he is now *witnessing* his volatility rather than only enduring it. Hospitalization is no longer a humiliating defeat but a recognized stabilization tool. He uses psychiatric resources, however reluctantly. The Sun King antagonist functions as a *projective test made flesh* — a rival Khonshu-avatar untroubled by conscience, doing exactly what Marc fears he is — and confronting him forces Marc to articulate, for the first time, what differentiates his violence from pure cult-religious psychopathy: it is the conscience, the doubt, the cost, the unwillingness to enjoy it.

**Cognitive style.** Increasingly *integrated under stress* — the alters cooperate more visibly, less competitively. Not fused, but federated.

**Self-concept.** *I am ill, and the illness has shape, and the shape has a use.* The moral framing returns but in mature form: he is not redeemed and not damned; he is responsible.

---

## XI. THE MACKAY / MIDNIGHT MISSION YEARS (~ages 52–55): SUBLIMATION AS LIFE — *Ministry from Fracture*

**Affect regulation.** The most mature configuration of his life. The Mission externalizes the regulating frame that the cape, the temple, the Avengers tenure, and the suit each provided in turn — but for the first time the frame is *prosocial in design rather than only in side-effect*. He provides for others what was never provided for him: a regulated, predictable, available figure who responds to crisis without being capsized by it. The act of *being that figure* down-regulates his own system in the process. This is genuine sublimation in the psychoanalytic sense — the trauma is doing work for others, and in the doing is metabolized.

**Cognitive style.** Pastoral-tact


## Psychiatric Assessment & Differential

# UATU DOSSIER — MARC SPECTOR / MOON KNIGHT
## Section 4: Psychiatric Assessment & Differential

---

### 4.0 Framing Caveats

Before any diagnostic schema is applied, three caveats must be entered into the file, because each one alters the read.

**First, the Khonshu Problem.** Marc Spector's clinical picture cannot be cleanly disentangled from the question of whether the Egyptian moon-god speaking to him is ontologically real within his universe. The available canonical evidence is, by deliberate authorial design, *non-falsifiable from the inside.* The Lemire/Smallwood arc (*Moon Knight* vol. 8) constructs an asylum frame in which every supernatural element collapses into psychiatric illness; the MacKay run (vol. 9) restores Khonshu as a discrete external agent capable of acting on other avatars (Hunter's Moon / Dr. Badr) who corroborate the experience. The dossier therefore proceeds along **two parallel tracks** wherever it matters: a *naturalistic track* (Khonshu as dissociated introject and psychotic-spectrum phenomenon) and a *consensus-reality track* (Khonshu as real but parasitic). The structure of the pathology is largely invariant across both; what changes is whether certain symptoms are coded as hallucination or as accurate perception of a hostile metaphysical agent. The clinician's responsibility is to note the divergence, not to resolve it.

**Second, the Longitudinal Problem.** This is fifty publication-years of behavior across roughly a dozen primary writers, each with a distinct interpretive lens. The diagnostic call must triangulate on the *invariants* — what persists across Moench, Dixon, Huston, Bendis, Ellis, Lemire, Bemis, and MacKay — rather than privilege any single era's framing. Invariants: identity multiplicity with amnestic barriers; mood-congruent persecutory/protective auditory and visual phenomena attributed to Khonshu; service-violence in white; intimacy avoidance with a stable small chosen family; depressive collapses in unstructured periods; substance-use relapses under chronic pain. These are the diagnostic bedrock.

**Third, the Forensic Problem.** Subject has a documented mercenary career involving lethal violence for hire. Any diagnostic frame must address whether his current pro-social functioning is sincere remission of a character-pathological pattern, or sincere continuity of a never-character-pathological self that took moral injury through bad employment. The evidence — exhaustively reviewed below — supports the latter.

---

### 4.1 Principal Diagnosis: Dissociative Identity Disorder (DSM-5 300.14 / ICD-11 6B64)

**Criterion A — Disruption of identity by two or more distinct personality states.** Satisfied at a level rarely seen outside textbook examples. The foundational triad — Marc Spector (depressive-aggressive core, holds guilt and rage and the mercenary memory), Steven Grant (financier; affable, articulate, capable of social registers Marc cannot access; holds competence, social grace, and a hypomanic-tinged charm), and Jake Lockley (cab-driver; coarse, vernacular, street-vigilant, holds nocturnal aggression and HUMINT skill, in later runs darker and frankly homicidal) — is documented from *Moon Knight* vol. 1 (Moench, 1980) forward. Each state carries its own:
- *Phenomenology* — voice pitch and prosody (Steven's polished East Coast finishing-school cadence; Jake's New York Hispanic-inflected street register; Marc's flatter, Midwestern-mercenary affect);
- *Motor signature* — Steven's upright, deliberate carriage versus Jake's hunched, kinetic, hand-talking; Marc's tight, combat-economical movement;
- *Skill differentials* — Steven's facility with finance, art, etiquette; Jake's facility with informants, gambling, street Spanish; Marc's facility with weapons and tactics. These are not stylistic flourishes; they are reliably distinguished by allies (Frenchie, Marlene, Gena) across decades;
- *Handwriting and signature differentials* (depicted explicitly in Lemire/Smallwood);
- *Preference structures* — Steven's wine and tailored clothing; Jake's diner coffee and street food; Marc's indifferent self-feeding.

Expansion-era alters (Bendis/Maleev, *Moon Knight* vol. 5) — the hallucinated Captain America, Wolverine, and Spider-Man — represent a **secondary fragmentation under decompensation**, in which the system recruited *external cultural templates* of heroism when the original alter triad could no longer organize Marc's pro-social violence. Diagnostically, this is not new personalities arising sui generis; it is the existing dissociative apparatus reaching for borrowed authority because the indigenous authorities (Steven, Jake, Khonshu) had become insufficient or untrustworthy. Bemis's "Sun King" and the further alter proliferation in his run represent a similar stress-driven elaboration.

**Criterion B — Recurrent gaps in recall.** Documented across the entire publication history. Marc cannot account for hours and sometimes days spent as Jake (Huston run is most explicit; Marc finds himself bloodied with no memory of the act); Steven's financial transactions occur without Marc's awareness; Marlene's testimony across runs is that Marc has frequently "lost" entire conversations. The amnesia is asymmetric and follows the classic DID pattern: alters often have one-way windows into Marc's experience while Marc has thicker walls.

**Criterion C — Clinically significant distress and impairment.** Catastrophically met. Romantic life: a thirty-plus-year inability to sustain proximity with Marlene Alraune, the most stable attachment of his adult life, attributable directly to her inability to know which Marc she is in bed with. Occupational: he has held no continuous identity-stable occupation; the alters *are* the occupations. Self-experience: subject describes himself as "broken," "crazy," "not a real person" across virtually every writer's run.

**Criterion D — Not a normal part of broadly accepted cultural or religious practice.** Met. The Jewish-American secular-Reform context of the Spector household does not authorize identity multiplicity. Khonshu-worship is not a community practice for Marc; it is private, idiosyncratic, and isolating.

**Criterion E — Not attributable to substance or other medical condition.** Met with the caveats below regarding TBI contribution.

**Etiology.** The classical DID etiological model — chronic, repetitive, inescapable childhood trauma in a developmentally vulnerable window — fits. Lemire's flashbacks and the Bemis/MacKay maternal-abuse retcons (a mother who was either mentally ill, abusive, or both, with Marc dissociating maternal violence to preserve the capacity to love her) place the originating fracture in early childhood, *years before* the Sudan event. The Khonshu encounter in the Temple is therefore correctly understood as a **consolidating and structuring event** for a pre-existing dissociative organization — not as the originating trauma. This matters diagnostically: it explains why the system is so elaborate (it had a head start), why it recruited a god (it needed an organizing principle for the multiple parts), and why "curing" Marc by removing Khonshu (Lemire arc; various antagonist attempts) produces collapse rather than integration.

**System organization.** Marc-self functions as the apparent host but is more properly described as the *guilt-bearing identity* in a system where executive function is distributed. Steven is the public-facing apparent normal part; Jake is the protector/persecutor in the van der Hart structural-dissociation sense — protector of the system, persecutor of those outside it. Khonshu, in the naturalistic reading, is a **persecutor-introject with grandiose-religious organization** — well-described in the DID literature, where a survivor of severe abuse internalizes an omnipotent figure that demands obedience, punishes deviation, and offers protection in exchange for service. The fit is exact.

---

### 4.2 Co-Occurring: Complex Post-Traumatic Stress Disorder (ICD-11 6B41)

The ICD-11 C-PTSD construct fits more cleanly than DSM-5 PTSD because it captures the **developmental layering** and the **disturbances in self-organization** that PTSD alone elides.

**PTSD-core symptoms:**
- *Re-experiencing:* Nightmares (Lemire run), intrusive flashbacks to Sudan, to combat in his Marine years, to specific kills (Huston run shows him flashing involuntarily mid-conversation); sensory triggers — desert heat, the specific sound of certain firearms, the smell of blood in sand — all canonical at various points.
- *Avoidance:* Behavioral (avoids hospitals; avoids his father's grave for years; avoids Chicago); cognitive (the dissociative architecture is itself the avoidance mechanism — the alters carry what Marc cannot).
- *Hyperarousal:* Chronic insomnia, exaggerated startle response, hypervigilance scaled to operational paranoia. Sleeps with weapons; clears rooms reflexively; reads rooflines and sightlines on entering any space.

**C-PTSD-specific Disturbances in Self-Organization:**
- *Affective dysregulation:* Either flat affect (Marc-self at rest) or explosive, often in the form of disproportionate violence — Bushman's scalping/face-removal is the textbook example; lower-grade examples saturate the canon.
- *Negative self-concept:* Documented across every writer. "I am not a good man." "I'm a killer who wears white." "There is something wrong with me." This is the affective baseline.
- *Disturbances in relationships:* The Marlene pattern is paradigmatic — approach, deepen, dissociate, withdraw, return. Frenchie tolerates it because Frenchie is a soldier who reads loyalty differently than intimacy. New attachments (Reese, Soldier in MacKay) are kept in defined operational roles.

**Etiology — multi-layered:**
1. *Developmental trauma* (maternal abuse; paternal helplessness in the face of it).
2. *Adolescent violence* (boxing — sanctioned head trauma plus a culture of pain endurance).
3. *Combat* (Marines — combat exposure, moral injury).
4. *Mercenary trauma* (commissioning of and participation in atrocity; the Sudan event is the apex but not the only event).
5. *Vigilante trauma* (chronic, ongoing, lifelong).

The five layers are not independent; each consolidated and re-traumatized the previous structure. The C-PTSD diagnosis is therefore correctly read as the *bed* on which the DID lies, not a separate condition co-occurring at random.

---

### 4.3 Co-Occurring: Major Depressive Disorder, Recurrent, Severe, With Mixed and Psychotic Features

**Episodic course over the canonical timeline:**
- *Pre-Huston withdrawal episode:* Months to years of immobility post-Bushman crippling event. Atrophic, sedentary, substance-using, suicidal in the passive sense (allowing the body to decay rather than active attempt — although the line between passive suicidality and Khonshu-deferred death is blurred).
- *Lemire asylum episode:* Catatonic stretches alternating with confused agitation; loss of capacity to recruit alter resources; collapse of the organizing narrative.
- *Post-resurrection episodes (MacKay):* Brief but acute; the resurrection itself appears to produce a depressive rebound, possibly because returning from death without the violent mission already structured around him removes the only thing that defends against the affective floor.

**Symptom inventory across episodes:** anhedonia (loss of even the joy of the hunt); hopelessness; psychomotor retardation in collapse-phases and agitation in mixed-phases; sleep disturbance (compounded by the baseline nocturnal pattern, so harder to detect); appetite loss (notable when Marlene is not present to feed him); suicidal ideation expressed almost entirely as *seeking lethal contact* with enemies, with the cape providing plausible deniability to himself and others.

**Dysthymic baseline.** Between major episodes, the Marc-self presents with persistent low-grade depression — flat affect, low hedonic capacity, ruminative self-condemnation. Steven and Jake do not display this; the affective load is concentrated in the host, by design. This is consistent with the DID system architecture: depression is *contained* in the part of the system that can bear it without losing function.

**"Psychotic features" qualifier.** Under the naturalistic reading, Khonshu's voice and visual presence intensify during depressive episodes — a classic mood-congruent psychotic feature. Under the consensus-reality reading, Khonshu opportunistically presses harder during Marc's depressive vulnerability. Both readings predict the same observable: Khonshu's salience increases when Marc is at his lowest.

---

### 4.4 Co-Occurring: Substance Use Disorders, In Variable Remission

**Alcohol Use Disorder, moderate, in sustained partial remission with periodic relapse.** Documented Huston run; reappears at intervals. The drinking is solitary, joyless, anesthetic — not social, not pleasure-seeking. Pattern is more consistent with self-medication of pain (physical and affective) than with primary addictive reward-seeking. He stops when the mission resumes; this is not a feature of severe AUD but of *instrumental* substance use in a man whose alternative coping mechanism (violent service) is highly effective when available.

**Opioid Use Disorder, moderate, in sustained remission with documented historical episode.** Huston run is explicit — analgesic use post-injury escalating into dependence. Subsequent runs reference the episode but do not depict active use. Risk of relapse remains elevated given the chronic pain substrate and the lifelong injury accumulation.

**Notably absent:** stimulants, hallucinogens, cannabis. The Jake-Lockley hypomanic productivity is endogenous (a state-switch phenomenon), not chemical. This absence is itself diagnostically informative — it argues against a primary addictive-spectrum disorder and toward instrumental, pain-driven use.

---

### 4.5 Probable Contributor: Major or Mild Neurocognitive Disorder Due to Traumatic Brain Injury (DSM-5 331.83 / chronic traumatic encephalopathy spectrum)

Subject has sustained head trauma at a rate and severity that would, in any naturalistic frame, produce significant cumulative neurocognitive sequelae:
- Adolescent and young-adult boxing.
- Marine combat.
- Mercenary engagements including the Sudan beating sufficient to be mistaken for death.
- Approximately five publication-decades of vigilante combat involving regular blunt-force cranial impact, with the cowl providing some but not complete protection.
- Multiple "deaths" with attendant anoxic insult.

**Clinical features attributable, in whole or in part, to TBI/CTE substrate:**
- Emotional dysregulation, particularly explosive aggression.
- Impulsivity in tactical contexts that contradicts his demonstrated planning capacity.
- Increasing vividness and intrusiveness of Khonshu phenomena across decades (the trajectory from voice-occasionally-heard in Moench to constant visually-present hallucination in Huston onward fits the progressive course of CTE-spectrum disorder as well as it fits worsening dissociative decompensation).
- Possible contribution to depressive episodes — affective disturbance is a documented feature of CTE.
- Sleep disturbance amplification.

**This diagnosis is contributory rather than primary.** Most of the psychiatric picture predates the bulk of cumulative TBI exposure. But it must be entered into the file as a *progressive complicator* — the substrate is unambiguously damaged, and any treatment planning that ignores the organic dimension will fail.

---

### 4.6 Differential — What Marc Spector Is Not, and Why

The differential is where most clinical errors regarding this subject have historically been made. Each rule-out below is substantiated, not asserted.

**4.6.1 Not Schizophrenia (DSM-5 295.90 / ICD-11 6A20).**

Rejected on multiple grounds.
- *Thought form is preserved.* Across all runs, Marc's discourse — even in florid Khonshu-haunted phases — retains logical structure, goal-directedness, and syntactic integrity. There is no derailment, no word salad, no loosening of associations, no neologisms.
- *Negative symptoms are absent.* Marc displays no flattening of the schizophrenic type (his flatness is depressive, mood-congruent, and reactive to circumstance); no avolition (he is, if anything, pathologically driven); no alogia; no asociality of the schizophrenic kind (his isolation is defensive and selective, not consequent on impaired social motivation).
- *Hallucinatory phenomena are mood- and trauma-congruent, narratively coherent, and embedded in an organized belief system* — features that argue against schizophrenia (where psychotic content is more often bizarre, fragmented, and ego-dystonic) and in favor of a dissociative or trauma-spectrum etiology.
- *Premorbid functioning was high.* Marine selection, CIA recruitment, and operational competence as a mercenary all indicate strong cognitive and executive baseline — inconsistent with the prodromal decline typical of schizophrenia.
- *Age of onset is wrong.* The originating fracture is childhood; the symptomatic consolidation is in early adulthood under combat and torture conditions, not in the late-adolescent to early-twenties window typical of schizophrenia, and not following the characteristic prodrome.
- *Response to "antipsychotic" containment is wrong.* The Lemire asylum arc, whatever else it depicts, shows that pharmacological suppression of the Khonshu phenomenon does not produce stabilization; it produces collapse — because the phenomenon is doing structural work in a dissociative architecture, not generating noise in a primary psychotic one.

**4.6.2 Not Schizoaffective Disorder (DSM-5 295.70 / ICD-11 6A21).**

Rejected because the psychotic-spectrum features are not present *independent* of mood and trauma triggers. There is no documented two-week period of Khonshu phenomena in the absence of mood disturbance or trauma cueing. The criterion fails.

**4.6.3 Not Bipolar I Disorder.**

The Steven-as-hypomanic / Marc-as-depressed contrast is superficially suggestive, but:
- The "manic" states are *dissociative state-switches,* not sustained mood episodes. They lack duration (Steven can be present for an hour or a week, but the timing tracks switching demands, not the seven-day manic floor or four-day hypomanic floor).
- They lack the characteristic sleep reduction, flight of ideas, distractibility, and goal-directed activity in the bipolar sense — Steven is focused and competent, not pressured and disorganized.
- They are *bounded by amnestic barriers,* which mood episodes are not.
- Bipolar II features on the *affective* side (the Marc-self alone) are reasonable and may co-exist as a minor accompaniment, but the diagnosis cannot bear the weight of the overall picture.

**4.6.4 Not Antisocial Personality Disorder (DSM-5 301.7).**

Rejected definitively, despite the mercenary history.
- *Conscience is intact and operative.* The entire arc of his adult life is guilt-organized. ASPD requires absence of remorse; subject is constituted of remorse.
- *Capacity for attachment is preserved.* Marlene, Frenchie, Gena and her sons, Reese, Soldier — these are real attachments, sustained over decades, defended at cost.
- *No childhood Conduct Disorder pattern* of the ASPD-precursor kind. The childhood violence that is suggested is reactive and self-protective in the trauma frame, not predatory.
- *The mercenary phase is moral injury cause, not character disorder evidence.* He left it under conditions that no antisocial individual leaves a profitable career under — at gunpoint, with a moral revolt against the killing of innocents.

**4.6.5 Not Narcissistic Personality Disorder (DSM-5 301.81).**

The Steven Grant alter exhibits narcissistic surface features — wealth display, social poise, a certain self-regard. But:
- *The host self is self-loathing, not grandiose.* The endogenous self-concept is the diagnostic floor.
- *Grandiosity is borrowed, not endogenous.* The Bendis-era recruitment of Captain America/Wolverine/Spider-Man as alters is precisely the move of a person who *cannot generate* internal grandiosity and must import it.
- *Empathy is preserved and operative,* particularly toward children, victims, and the mentally ill — directly contradicting the empathic deficit criterion.

**4.6.6 Not Borderline Personality Disorder (DSM-5 301.83).**

The overlap is real (identity disturbance; splitting; impulsivity; recurrent self-damaging behavior). The distinction is structural:
- *BPD identity disturbance is diffuse and affect-driven;* subject's identity disturbance is *discretely organized into named, skill-differentiated states with amnestic barriers.* These are diagnostically different phenomena.
- *BPD relational pattern is idealize/devalue with abandonment terror.* Subject's relational pattern is *avoidant-protective* — he withdraws *to protect the other from him,* and tolerates abandonment as deserved rather than panics against it.
- *Affective instability in BPD is moment-to-moment and reactive to interpersonal cues.* Subject's affective shifts are state-bounded and tied to alter switches.

A BPD-spectrum co-feature could be argued for the Marc-self in isolation; the diagnosis as a whole cannot be sustained.

**4.6.7 Not Malingering or Factitious Disorder.**

Rejected on the standard secondary-gain analysis. The alters cost him love, stability, occupational coherence, legal standing, and on several occasions his liberty. There is no rational secondary gain. The system is genuinely *trying to function*; that the function it has organized is violent service to a moon-god is a comment on the resources available, not on the sincerity of the structure.

**4.6.8 Not Substance/Medication-Induced Psychotic or Dissociative Disorder.**

The Khonshu phenomena and the alter system predate and outlast any documented substance use. Substance use is a contributor in specific eras, not the etiology.

**4.6.9 Not Religious or Spiritual Problem (DSM-5 V62.89), as primary frame.**

Even under the consensus-reality reading where Khonshu is real, the *Marc-Khonshu relationship* is structurally abusive — coercive, conditional, punitive, and degrading. A genuine religious-problem frame (which is appropriate for distress arising from sincere faith within a non-pathological structure) does not accommodate the degree of psychiatric morbidity present. This is a coded relationship, and the co


## Behavioral Atlas

# UATU DOSSIER — MARC SPECTOR / MOON KNIGHT
## SECTION VI: BEHAVIORAL ATLAS

A longitudinal inventory of how the subject occupies space, distributes affect, makes decisions, and betrays interior state across every observed condition. Compiled from forty-eight years of canonical observation (1975–present), cross-indexed against the dissociative, post-traumatic, and neurocognitive substrate established in Sections III–IV. Behaviors are catalogued not as character color but as *signals* — each one a data point a long-running file would log and trend.

---

### 1. BASELINE / CALM — THE RARE CONDITION

True calm is the subject's least frequent state. When observed (safe-house downtime, post-mission decompression, the brief plateaus of the Ellis/Shalvey period, certain Midnight Mission mornings in the MacKay run), it presents as follows:

- **Posture.** Sits forward, not back. Even in his own living rooms, the spine does not commit to furniture; weight stays over the balls of the feet, hands on thighs or wrapped around a mug. He does not lounge. The single canonical exception is when Marlene is present and asleep against him, at which point he goes very still rather than relaxed — a stillness that registers to outside observers as peace and to clinical observation as freeze.
- **Gaze pattern.** Even in calm, the eyes perform a slow circuit of room exits every 40–90 seconds. He clocks windows, doors, sightlines, and the position of any object that could serve as a weapon or projectile. He does this so consistently that Frenchie has, in dialogue, finished the sweep for him.
- **Hands.** When unoccupied, the right hand will find the left wrist and grip it — a self-soothing pressure that mimics the gauntlets he wears in costume. When this hand-on-wrist hold appears in civilian clothes, it is a reliable indicator that an alter-shift is being suppressed.
- **Speech.** Slow, low, dry. He uses fewer words in calm than in stress — the inverse of most subjects. Humor surfaces here and almost nowhere else; it is self-deprecating, frequently Jewish-inflected (a Borscht Belt cadence the MacKay run leans into), and tends to land just before he changes the subject away from himself.
- **Eating.** Eats when reminded. Prefers high-protein, single-ingredient foods (eggs, steak, fish), eaten standing or at a counter, rarely at a table. Coffee black, constantly. He has been observed across multiple runs to forget meals entirely for 24–36 hours and then eat a single enormous one, a pattern consistent with both depressive anhedonia and the operational rhythms of his mercenary years.
- **Sleep.** Brief, fragmented, almost never in a bed when alone. Couches, chairs, floor. When in a bed with Marlene, sleeps on his back, arms at his sides, on the side of the bed nearest the door. Wakes at any change in ambient sound; recovers consciousness in under two seconds with full situational orientation — a Marine residue compounded by paranoia.
- **Dress.** In private, dark T-shirt, dark trousers, boots laced. The white of the costume is reserved for the work; he does not wear white casually. The wallet is in a front pocket, not a back pocket. Keys clipped, not loose.

These calm-state behaviors are not the absence of vigilance; they are vigilance operating at its lowest sustainable idle. The subject has no observable *off* state.

---

### 2. PRE-MISSION RITUAL — THE TRANSITION

Across every era in which an operational sequence has been depicted in detail (Moench's Bushman pursuit arcs, Huston's return, Ellis's case files, MacKay's nightly Mission shifts), a recognizable pre-mission rhythm has been logged. The order is near-invariant; the ritual is itself a containment vessel for the alter-shift.

1. **Withdrawal from civilian company.** He leaves the room without explanation. Marlene and Frenchie no longer ask where he is going; Reese has been observed learning the same restraint.
2. **Physical preparation in silence.** Wraps hands (boxing legacy). Inspects gear in a fixed order — crescent darts, truncheon, grappling line, throwing crescents, cowl — touching each item once even when the inventory has not changed.
3. **The mirror moment.** He looks at himself in the suit, briefly, and the face that looks back is not always the one that put it on. Sienkiewicz drew this; Smallwood drew this; multiple artists have independently rendered the same beat. The mirror is the threshold; the alter that exits the room is rarely the one that entered it.
4. **A line spoken aloud, to no one.** Some variant of *"Tonight"* or *"All right"* or, in the Khonshu-loud periods, an address to the god. This is the verbal handoff.
5. **Exit through a window or rooftop, not a door,** even when a door would be operationally equivalent. The vigilante is not allowed to use the door of the man.

---

### 3. UNDER ACUTE STRESS — COMBAT AND PURSUIT

- **Pain response.** Markedly blunted. Logs a hit with a small exhalation rather than a vocalization. When struck hard enough to draw an audible reaction, the sound is almost always a short laugh — diagnostic of dissociation under impact, not bravado.
- **Switching under fire.** When physically overmatched, Jake surfaces — gait widens, weight drops, strikes shift from boxing (jab-cross, hooks, structured combinations) to *street* (head-butts, eye-gouges, joint breaks, improvised weapons, biting in at least two logged incidents). When tactically overmatched (multiple opponents, complex environment), Steven surfaces — voice gentles, planning verbalizes, he begins narrating options aloud in complete sentences. The switch is observable to trained eyes within two to three seconds.
- **Use of the cape.** The cape is not theater; it is a *disorientation tool* and a *withdrawal screen.* He uses it to break line of sight before repositioning, almost never as a flourish. When he does flourish it, he is performing for a witness — usually a child, occasionally a frightened civilian he wants to comfort by looking mythic.
- **Restraint pattern toward enemies.** Disproportionate. He inflicts more damage than neutralization requires, and almost always lands one final blow after the opponent is non-threatening — a punctuation, often to the face. The face is where he marks his work; Bushman set the template and he has never broken it. Cracked teeth, broken orbital bones, and forehead lacerations recur in the wakes of his fights at a rate well above any other Marvel street-level operator.
- **Verbal output during violence.** Minimal as Marc. Increases as Jake (taunts, profanity, dark jokes). Almost continuous as Steven (running commentary). The voice profile alone allows remote identification of which alter is on deck during an op.
- **Decision speed.** Faster than his peers. Where Daredevil deliberates and Punisher pre-plans, the subject *commits* — he selects a course inside the first half-second of engagement and corrects mid-motion. This produces extraordinary results when his read is correct and catastrophic ones when it is wrong; he has been knocked unconscious and seriously injured more often than any non-powered street operator of comparable tenure.
- **Tolerance for own injury during engagement.** Effectively infinite until the objective is met, at which point the body collapses on a delay. Frenchie has had to physically catch him after the moment-of-completion in at least four logged incidents across the Moench and Huston runs. This is not stoicism; it is dissociation from somatic feedback channels that come back online only when the alter releases the body.

---

### 4. THREAT TO OTHERS — THE OVERRIDE CONDITION

When a third party — particularly a child, a woman in immediate danger, an elderly person, or a visibly mentally ill person — is the target of violence in his line of sight, every rule above is overwritten.

- **Tactical sense degrades to near-zero.** He will cross open ground, ignore cover, and engage numerically superior opposition without weighing odds. Multiple writers have used this as a plot driver because it is the most reliably exploitable trait he has. A competent enemy who has studied him can bait him with a hostage every time.
- **The voice drops an octave** and acquires a flat affect that is *not* any of the named alters — it is something colder underneath them. Allies have described this voice as the moment they become genuinely frightened of him.
- **Mercy circuit disengages.** The post-neutralization punctuation blow (see above) becomes a sequence. He has had to be pulled off opponents by Frenchie, by Marlene, by Tigra during his Avengers tenure, and by Reese in the MacKay run.
- **Post-event behavior.** He will physically place himself between the victim and the threat for several minutes after the threat is neutralized, often crouching to be at the victim's eye level if the victim is a child, and speaking in a register no other condition elicits — quiet, slow, plain, almost rabbinical. This is the closest the subject ever comes to displaying his father's voice.

---

### 5. INTIMACY — THE CONDITION HE CANNOT SUSTAIN
